The legal defense of set-off ( above ) was originally introduced to prevent the unfair हालात whereby a व्यक्ति ( `` पार्टी a '' ) जो owed धन to another ( `` पार्टी b '' ) could be भेजा to कर्जदार थाना, despite the fact that Party B also owed money to Party A.
The law यूँ allows दोनो पार्टियों to टालना भुगतान जबतक उनके संबंधित claims have been heard in court.
Upon judgment, both claims are बुझे और replaced by a सिंगल जाल योग owing ( e.g. if पार्टी a owes पार्टी b 100 और पार्टी b owes पार्टी a 105, the दो रकम हैं नियत बंद and replaced with a single obligation of 5 from Party B to Party A ).
Set-off can also be incorporated by contractual अनुबंध so कि, जहाँ a पार्टी मूलभूत, the परस्पर amounts owing हैं automatically set off and extinguished.
In certain jurisdictions ( including the uk ), set-off takes प्लेस automatically upon the insolvency of a company.
This means that, लिये प्रत्येक पार्टी जिससे is दोनो a creditor और debtor of the insolvent कम्पनी, परस्पर debts हैं set-off विरूद्ध प्रत्येक अन्य, और तब either the दिवालिया 's creditor can अर्जी the संतुलन in the दिवालियापन or the trustee in bankruptcy can ask for the balance remaining to be paid, depending on which side owed the most.
This has been criticized as an undeclared सुरक्षा ब्याज कि violates the principle of pari passu.
The alternative, where a creditor रै to अदा सब इसके debts, लकिन प्राप्त तभी a सीमित portion of the leftover moneys that other unsecured creditors get, poses the danger of 'knock-on ' insolvencies.
The right to set off is particularly important when reporting a बैंको 's विकिरणों to नियामक अधिकारियों.
The situation where a bank has to report that it has lent a large sum to a borrower ( and is therefore exposed, because there is a risk that the borrower might डिफॉल्ट thereby अग्रणी to the घाटा of the बैंको 's or इसके जमाकर्ताओं ' धन ) is यूँ replaced ( जहाँ the बैंको रै लिया सुरक्षा over साझा or प्रतिभूति of the borrower ) साथ an एक्सपोज़र of the money lent minus the value of the security taken.

Conventional पीसीआई ( पीसीआई is an initialism formed इससे परिधीय घटक इंटरकनेक्ट, भाग of the पीसीआई लोकल बस मानक और प्रायः shortened to बस पीसीआई ) is a local computer bus for attaching hardware devices in a computer.
The PCI bus supports the functions मिला on a प्रोसेसर बस, लकिन in a मानकीकृत स्वरूप कि is स्वतंत्र of कोई particular प्रोसेसर.
Devices connected to the बस appear to the प्रोसेसर to be कनेक्ट सीधे to the प्रोसेसर बस, और हैं आबंटित addresses in the processor 's address space.
Attached devices can take either the रूप of an एकीकृत सर्किट fitted onto the मदरबोर्ड itself, पुकारा a planar यंत्र in the पीसीआई specification, or an expansion card that fits into a slot.
The PCI Local Bus was first implemented in IBM PC compatibles, जहाँ it विस्थापित the संयोजन of isa प्लस एक vesa Local Bus as the bus configuration.
It has subsequently महरूम अपनाया लिये अन्य computer types.
PCI and PCI-X are being replaced by PCI Express, but, सबसे motherboards हैं स्टिल बना साथ एक or अधिक पीसीआई स्लॉट, जिससे हैं sufficient for many uses.
The PCI specification कवर the शारीरिक आकार of the बस ( सहित the आकार और अंतरण of the सर्किट फलक किनारे विद्युत contacts ), electrical characteristics, bus timing, and protocols.
The specification can be खरीदा इससे the पीसीआई Special Interest Group ( PCI-SIG ).
Typical PCI cards used in PCs include : network cards, ध्वनि ताश, modems, अतिरिक्त पोर्ट ऐसे as usb or सीरियल, tv ट्यूनर ताश and disk controllers.
PCI video cards replaced ISA और vesa ताश, जबतक growing बैंडविड्थ आवश्यकताएँ outgrew the सामर्थ्य of पीसीआई ; the पसन्दीदा इंटरफ़ेस लिये वीडियो ताश became अगप, और तब पीसीआई Express.
PCI वीडियो ताश remain उपलब्धियाँ लिये उपयोग साथ बूढ़ा pcs बगैर अगप or पीसीआई एक्स्प्रेस slots.
Many devices previously provided on पीसीआई विस्तार ताश हैं अभी commonly एकीकृत onto motherboards or available in universal serial bus and PCI Express versions.
Caffeine is a कड़वा, श्वेत crystalline xanthine एल्कलॉएड कि acts as a stimulant drug.
Caffeine is found in varying quantities in the seeds, leaves, and fruit of कुछ पौधे, जहाँ it अधिनियमों as a प्राकृतिक कीटनाशक कि paralyzes और मारता निश्चित कीट feeding on the पौधे, as खूब as बढ़ाना the reward memory of pollinators.
It is most commonly consumed by humans in infusions extracted from the seed of the coffee संयंत्र और the पत्ते of the चाय बुश, as खूब as इससे विभिन्न भोजन और पेय containing उत्पाद निकला from the kola nut.
Other स्त्रोत शामिल yerba maté, guarana जामुन, guayusa, and the yaupon holly.
In humans, caffeine acts as a central nervous प्रणाली उत्तेजक, temporarily warding बंद drowsiness और restoring alertness.
It is the world 's most widely consumed psychoactive drug, but unlike many other psychoactive substances, it is विधिक और unregulated in nearly सब भाग of the संसार.
Beverages containing caffeine, ऐसे as कॉफी, चाय, नरम पेय, और उर्जा पेय, आनंद great popularity.
In North अमेरिका, 90 % of वयस्कों consume कैफीन रोज़.
Part of the reason caffeine is classified by the Food and Drug प्रशासन as ग्रा ( generally पहचाना as सुरक्षित ) is कि विषाक्त doses ( over 10 गामा ) हैं much higher than typically used doses ( less than 500 milligrams ).
Ordinary consumption can have low health risks, भी जब carried on लिये सालो – वहीँ may be a modest सुरक्षात्मक प्रभाव विरूद्ध कुछ रोगों, सहित parkinsons Disease, and certain types of cancer.
Caffeine can have दोनो धनात्मक और ऋणात्मक प्रभाव on चिंता disorders.
Some people experience sleep disruption if they consume caffeine, especially दौरान the संध्या घंटों, लकिन अन्य दिखाएँ छोटी disturbance और the प्रभाव of कैफीन on sleep is highly variable.
Evidence of a रिस्क to गर्भावस्था is equivocal, लकिन कुछ अधिकारियों have concluded कि दूरदर्शी सलाह is लिये गर्भवती महिलाओं to limit consumption to the equivalent of two cups of coffee per day or less.
The American Congress of Obstetricians and Gynecologists ( ACOG ) concluded in 2010 कि कैफीन खपत is सुरक्षित up to 200 mg प्रति दिन in गर्भवती women.
Caffeine has pressor and mild diuretic effects when administered to people who are not used to it, but regular उपयोक्ता develop a सहिष्णुता to इस प्रभाव, और अध्ययन have generally विफल to support the आम ख़्याल कि ordinary खपत contributes significantly to dehydration.
साथ भारी उपयोग, सहिष्णुता develops rapidly to autonomic प्रभाव ऐसे as elevated दिल रेट और मांसपेशी twitching, but not to the cognitive or arousal effects of caffeine.
The degree to which caffeine can produce clinically significant शारीरिक और दिमागी dependence remains a विषय of विवाद in the चिकित्सा साहित्य.

An automobile, autocar, मोटर car or car is a wheeled मोटर गाडी प्रयुक्त लिये transporting यात्री, जिससे also carries its own engine or motor.
Most definitions of the term specify that automobiles are designed to चलाएं primarily on सड़कें, to have seating लिये एक to आठ लोगों, to typically have चार पहियों, और to be constructed प्रधानतया for the transport of people rather than goods.

Kennedy defeated Vice President and रिपब्लिकन प्रत्याशी रिचर्ड निक्सन in the 1960 u.S. presidential election.
At 43 years of age, he is the youngest to have महरूम निर्वाचित to the दफ्तर, the second-youngest अध्यक्ष ( बाद थियोडोर रूज़वेल्ट ), और the पहला person born in the 20th century to serve as president.

The Kennedy administration adopted the policy of the रणनीतिक हैमलेट कार्यक्रम जिससे थी implemented by the दक्षिण वियतनामी सरकारी.

A Fire Alarm Control Panel ( FACP ), or आग सचेतक कंट्रोल ईकाई ( facu ), is the controlling घटक of a Fire Alarm System.
The panel receives information from environmental सेंसर designed to detect परिवर्तन संबद्ध साथ आग, मॉनीटर उनके operational अखंडता और provides लिये automatic control of equipment, and transmission of information necessary to prepare the facility for fire based on a predetermined sequence.
The panel may also supply electrical उर्जा to operate कोई संबद्ध सेंसर, कंट्रोल, ट्रांसमीटर, or relay.
There are four basic types of panels : coded panels, conventional panels, addressable panels, और मल्टीप्लेक्स प्रणालियों.

Black Swan is a 2010 American मनोवैज्ञानिक थ्रिलर और हॉरर फिल्मी निर्देशित by डैरेन aronofsky और अभिनीत नताली Portman, Vincent Cassel, and Mila Kunis.
The plot revolves around a उत्पादन of tchaikovsky 's swan झील बैले by a prestigious नई यॉर्क नगर company.
The production requires a नर्तकी to खेल the निर्दोष और नाजुक श्वेत swan, लिये जिससे the वचनबद्ध नर्तकी नीना ( पोर्टमैन ) is a पूर्ण अनुरूप, as खूब as the dark and sensual Black Swan, which are qualities embodied by the new arrival Lily ( Kunis ).
Nina is overwhelmed by a अहसास of immense दबाव जब वो पाता herself स्पर्धा लिये the भाग, causing उसके to खोना उसके tenuous पकड़ on reality and descend into a living nightmare.
Aronofsky conceived the आधार by connecting उसके viewings of a उत्पादन of swan झील साथ an unrealized पटकथा परिचय understudies and the notion of being haunted by a double, similar to the folklore surrounding doppelgängers.
Aronofsky cites Fyodor दोस्तोयेव्स्की 's `` the दोगुना `` as another inspiration for the film.
The director also considered Black Swan a साथी टुकड़ा to उसके 2008 फिल्मी the पहलवान, साथ दोनो films involving demanding performances for different kinds of art.
He and Portman first discussed the प्रोजेक्ट in 2000, और बाद a ब्रैड अनुलग्नक to सार्वभौमिक studios, ब्लैक swan थी produced in New York City in 2009 by Fox Searchlight Pictures.
Portman and Kunis trained in ballet for several months prior to फिल्मांकन, और notable आंकड़े इससे the बैले संसार helped साथ फिल्मी उत्पादन to आकार the ballet presentation.

The world’s पहला ice-calorimeter, प्रयुक्त in the शीत of 1782-83, by एंटोनी लाव्वाज़्ये और pierre-simon लाप्लास, to determine the ऊष्मा शामिल in various chemical changes ; calculations which were based on Joseph Black ’s prior discovery of latent heat.
These experiments mark the न्यास of thermochemistry.
A ऊष्मामापी ( इससे लैटिन calor, अर्थ ऊष्मा ) is an ऑब्जेक्ट प्रयुक्त लिये कैलोरीमिति, or the प्रक्रम of measuring the heat of chemical reactions or physical changes as well as heat capacity.
Differential scanning calorimeters, समतापी microcalorimeters, titration calorimeters और त्वरित रेट calorimeters हैं among the सबसे common types.
A simple calorimeter just consists of a थर्मामीटर संलग्न to a मेटल संग्राहक full of water suspended above a combustion chamber.
To find the enthalpy change per mole of a substance A in a reaction between दो substances a और b, the substances हैं added to a ऊष्मामापी और the आरंभिक और फाइनल temperatures ( पहले the प्रतिक्रिया started and after it has finished ) are noted.

dividing the उर्जा बदलें by कैसा अनेक औज़ार of a were present gives its enthalpy change of reaction.
This method is used primarily in अकादमिक शिक्षण as it describes the सिद्धान्त of कैलोरीमिति.

Flip-flops ( also called zōri, thongs, jandals, or a किस्में of अन्य names throughout the संसार ) हैं a प्रकार of open-toed चन्दन typically worn in कैज़ुअल situations, such as outside or at the beach.

The law of general average is a legal principle of maritime law according to which all parties in a sea venture proportionally share any losses resulting इससे a voluntary बलिदान of भाग of the जलयान or कार्गो to सहेजें the पूरे in an आपात.
In the exigencies of hazards faced at sea, crew members often have अनमोल छोटी समय in जिससे to determine precisely जिनकी कार्गो वे हैं jettisoning.
Thus, to avoid quarrelling that could बर्बाद मूल्यवान समय, वहीँ arose the निष्पक्ष अभ्यास whereby सब the व्यापारियों जिनकी कार्गो उतरा सकुशल होता be called on to contribute a portion, based upon a share or percentage, to the merchant or merchants whose goods had been tossed overboard to avert imminent peril.
While general average traces its origins in ancient maritime law, स्टिल it remains भाग of the admiralty विधि of most countries.
The first संहिताकरण of सामान्य औसत थी the यॉर्क antwerp Rules of 1890.

General average requires three elements which हैं clearly stated by mr. इंसाफ grier in बर्नार्ड v. आदमs:
`` 1st.
A common danger : a danger in which vessel, cargo and crew all participate ; a danger imminent and जाहिर 'inevitable, ' मगर by voluntarily रूष्ट the घाटा of a portion of the पूरे to सहेजें the शेष. ''
`` 2nd. There must be a voluntary jettison, jactus, or casting away, of some portion of the संयुक्त चिंता लिये the purpose of बचने इस निकट peril, periculi imminentis evitandi causa, or, in अन्य शब्द, a ट्रांसफ़र of the peril from the whole to a particular portion of the whole. ''
`` 3rd.
This attempt to avoid the निकट आम peril जरूर be successful ''.

A टीकाकरण अनुसूची is a श्रेणी of vaccinations, सहित the समय of all doses, which may be either recommended or compulsory, depending on the country of residence.
A vaccine is an antigenic preparation used to produce active immunity to a बीमारी, in अनुक्रम to prevent or reduce the प्रभाव of संक्रमण by कोई प्राकृतिक or `` जंगली '' pathogen.

For example, टेटनस टीका boosters हैं प्रायः अनुशंसित every 10 years.

Over the past two decades, the recommended vaccination अनुसूची रै grown rapidly और become अधिक जटिल as अनेक नई टीके have been developed.

This difference is due to the निम्नतर लागत of स्वास्थ्य परवाह, the निम्नतर लागत of अनेक टीके provided to विकासशील राष्ट्र, और कि अधिक महंगी vaccines, often for less common diseases, are not utilized.

it is कहा कि if the आइलैंडर्स हैं नहीं celebrating it, then they are preparing for it, while reminiscing about the past year 's festival.
The heart of the musical जश्न रै महरूम कैलिप्सो ; recently सोका रै replaced कैलिप्सो as the most celebrated type of music.
वेशभूषा, stickfighting और limbo प्रतियोगिताओं हैं भी महत्वपूर्ण components of the festival.
Carnival as it is मनाये in त्रिनिदाद और Tobago is also celebrated in cities worldwide.
These सहित टोरंटो 's caribana, मियामी 's मियामी कार्निवल, ह्यूस्टन carifest, लंदन 's नॉटिंग हिल कार्निवल as खूब as नई York City 's Labor Day Carnival to name a few.
Carnival was created when West African slaves mimicked उनके फ्रेंच स्वामी जो जहाँ ज्ञात लिये उनके lavish वेशभूषा गेंदें.
Forbidden to partake in these festivities and confined to their quarters, स्लेव संयुक्त तत्व इससे उनके अपना संस्कृतियों to उनके निपुण 's fete.
Hence the creation of characters such as Jab jab or jab molassie ( शैतानों ), मध्यरात्रि लुटेरों, imps, lagahroo, soucouyant, La Diablesse and Demons.
With the abolition of slavery in 1838, freed Africans took their version of कार्निवल to the गलियों through अभिव्यक्ति of ड्रम, riddim भाग जैसे tamboo बाँसुरी और as प्रत्येक नई अप्रवासी जनसांख्यिकी डाला त्रिनिदाद, कार्निवल विकसित into कया we know today.

Under the United States Constitution, the अध्यक्ष of the संयुक्त राज्य is the सिर of राज्य और सिर of सरकारी of the United States.
As chief of the executive branch and head of the federal सरकारी as a पूरे, the प्रेसिडेंसी is the उच्चतम राजनैतिक दफ्तर in the संयुक्त राज्य by influence और मान्यता.
The president is also the commander-in-chief of the संयुक्त राज्य हथियारबंद शक्तियां.
The president is indirectly निर्वाचित to a four-year पद by an चुनावी कॉलेज ( or by the हाउस of प्रतिनिधि should the Electoral College fail to award an absolute majority of votes to any person ).
Since the ratification of the Twenty-second Amendment to the United States Constitution in 1951, no person may be elected President more than twice, और no एक जो रै परोसा अधिक than दो सालो of a पद to जिससे किसी else थी निर्वाचित may be निर्वाचित अधिक than once.
Upon the death, resignation, or हटाना इससे दफ्तर of an लाज़िम अध्यक्ष, the वाइस अध्यक्ष assumes the office.
The President must be at least 35 years of आयु और a `` प्राकृतिक born '' नागरिक of the संयुक्त States.
This list शामिल तभी those व्यक्तियों जो यहूद sworn into दफ्तर as president following the ratification of the United States Constitution, which took effect on March 4, 1789.
For American नेताओ पहले इस अनुसमर्थन, देखिए अध्यक्ष of the महाद्वीपीय Congress.

वहीँ have महरूम 43 लोगों sworn into दफ्तर, और 44 presidencies, as ग्रोवर क्लीवलैंड परोसा दो non-consecutive terms and is counted chronologically as both the 22nd and 24th president.
Of the individuals elected as president, four died in office of natural causes ( William Henry Harrison, Zachary Taylor, Warren G. Harding, and Franklin D. रूज़वेल्ट ), चार यहूद assassinated ( अब्राहम lincoln, जेम्स A. गारफ़ील्ड, विलियम mckinley, और जॉन F. कैनेडी ) and one resigned ( Richard Nixon ).
George Washington, the first president, थी उदघाटन in 1789 बाद a सर्वसम्मत vote of the चुनावी कॉलेज.
William Henry Harrison spent the shortest time in office साथ 32 दिनों in 1841, और फ्रैंकलिन D. रूज़वेल्ट खर्च the longest साथ over बारह सालो, लकिन died shortly into उसके चौथी पद in 1945.
He is the only president to serve more than two terms, and a constitutional amendment, affecting राष्ट्रपतियों बाद हैरी ट्रूमैन, थी passed to सीमा the क्रमांक of टाइम्स an individual can be elected president.
एंड्रयू जैक्सन, the सातवाँ अध्यक्ष, थी the पहला to be निर्वाचित by मेन of सब वर्ग in 1828 after most laws barring non-land-owners from voting were repealed.

History records four राष्ट्रपतियों – जॉन q एडम्स, रदरफोर्ड B. हेज़, बेंजामिन हैरिसन और जार्ज W. बुश – जो खोया the popular vote but assumed office.

Utah ( or ) ( arapaho : wo'tééneihí ' ) is a राज्य in the Western United States.
It became the 45th राज्य admitted to the संघ on January 4, 1896.
Utah is the 13th-largest, the 34th-most populous, और the 10th-least-densely आबादी of the 50 United States.

It भी छू a कोने of नई मैक्सिको on the southeast.
Utah is the most religiously समरूप राज्य in the Union.
Approximately 63 % of Utahns are reported to be members of The गिरिजाघर of यीशु मसीह of latter-day संतो or lds ( mormons ), जिससे greatly influences Utah culture and daily life.

The state is a center of परिवहन, शिक्षा, सूचना प्रौद्योगिकी और शोध, सरकारी सेवाएं, खनन, और a major tourist destination for outdoor recreation.
According to the u.S. जनसांख्यिकी ब्यूरो 's जनसांख्यिकी estimates, Utah is the fifth fastest-growing state in the United States as of 2012.
St. George, was the fastest–growing महानगर क्षेत्रफल in the संयुक्त States from 2000 to 2005.

The tanakh (, or ; भी tenakh, tenak, tanach ) is a name used in Judaism for the canon of the Hebrew Bible.
The Tanakh is भी ज्ञात as the masoretic टेक्स्ट or the miqra.
The name is an acronym formed from the initial Hebrew letters of the Masoretic Text 's three traditional subdivisions : the तोरा ( `` शिक्षण '', भी ज्ञात as the पाँच किताबे of मूसा ), nevi'im ( `` नबियों '' ) और ketuvim ( `` कृतियाँ '' ) —hence TaNaKh.
The name `` Miqra '' ( מקרא ), अर्थ `` कि जिससे is पढ़ा '', is an वैकल्पिक यहूदी term for the Tanakh.
The books of the tanakh यहूद relayed साथ an accompanying मौखिक परंपरा passed on by प्रत्येक पीढी, called the Oral Torah.

Driving under the influence ( DUI ), driving while intoxicated ( DWI ), drunken driving, drunk driving, drink ड्राइविंग, ऑपरेटिंग अंतर्गत the influence, पीने और ड्राइविंग, or impaired ड्राइविंग is the अपराधों of ड्राइविंग a मोटर गाडी साथ रक्त स्तर of दारू in excess of a विधिक सीमा ( `` Blood Alcohol Content '', or `` BAC '' ).
समान regulations कवर ड्राइविंग or ऑपरेटिंग निश्चित प्रकार of मशीनरी जबकि प्रभावित by पीने दारू or taking other drugs, including, but not limited to prescription drugs.
इस is a दण्ड ठोकर in most nations.
convictions do नहीं necessarily involve actual driving of the vehicle.
in सबसे jurisdictions a मापन ऐसे as a रक्त दारू सामग्री ( bac ) in excess of a विशिष्ट दहलीज स्तर, such as 0.05 % or 0.08 % defines the offense, with no need to prove impairment or being under the influence of alcohol.
In some jurisdictions, वहीँ is an क्रोधित श्रेणी of the ठोकर at a higher level e.g. 0.12 %.
In most countries, anyone who is convicted of injuring or killing someone जबकि अंतर्गत the influence of दारू or दवाएँ can be heavily fined, as in फ़्रांस, in जोड to होने दिए a lengthy थाना sentence.
Some jobs have their own नियम और bac हद, लिये उदाहरण वाणिज्यिक पायलट, और the संघीय रेलरोड प्रशासन in the संयुक्त राज्य रै a 0.04 % limit for train crew.
Some jurisdictions have multiple levels of BAC ; for example, the state of कैलिफ़ोर्निया रै a 0.08 % bac सीमा, जिससे is lowered to 0.04 % if the ऑपरेटर holds a commercial driver 's license.
The California BAC limit is 0.01 % for those younger than 21 सालो of आयु और those on परिवीक्षा लिये a पिछला dui conviction.
Some large corporations have their अपना नियम ; संघ प्रशांत रेलरोड रै उनके अपना bac सीमा of 0.02 % कि, if violated दौरान a यादृच्छिक परीक्षण or a for-cause परीक्षण — लिये उदाहरण, बाद a traffic accident — can result in termination of employment with no chance of future re-hire.
Many states in the U.S. and provinces in कनाडा have अपनाया सच्चाई in sentencing कानून कि enforce सख्त दिशानिर्देश on sentencing, differing इससे पिछला practice where prison time was reduced or suspended after sentencing had been issued.
Some jurisdictions have न्यायिक दिशानिर्देश requiring a अनिवार्य न्यूनतम वाक्य.

The specific criminal offense may be called, depending on the jurisdiction, driving under the influence [ of alcohol or other drugs ] ( DUI ), driving under intense influence ( duii ), ड्राइविंग जबकि intoxicated ( dwi ), ऑपरेटिंग अंतर्गत the influence ( oui ) ऑपरेटिंग जबकि intoxicated ( owi ), ऑपरेटिंग a मोटर गाडी जबकि intoxicated ( omvi ), ड्राइविंग अंतर्गत the संयुक्त influence of alcohol and/or other drugs, driving under the influence per se or drunk in charge [ of a vehicle ].
Many such laws apply भी to motorcycling, बोटिंग, piloting वायुयान, उपयोग of motile फार्म उपकरण ऐसे as tractors और combines, सवारी घोड़े or ड्राइविंग a horse-drawn vehicle, or bicycling, possibly with different BAC level than driving.
In some jurisdictions वहीँ हैं पृथक आरोप depending on the गाडी प्रयुक्त, ऐसे as bwi ( bicycling जबकि intoxicated ), which may carry a lighter sentence.

Law enforcement in the United राज्य is एक of तीन प्रमुख components of the दण्ड इंसाफ प्रणाली of the संयुक्त राज्य, along with courts and corrections.
Although there exists an inherent interrelatedness between the अलग समूह कि मेक up the दण्ड इंसाफ प्रणाली आधारित on उनके अपराधों deterrence purpose, each component operates independently from one another.
However, the न्यायपालिका is vested साथ the शक्ति to मेक विधिक determinations regarding the conduct of the other two components.
Apart from maintaining order and service functions, the purpose of policing is the छानबीन of suspected दण्ड कार्यकलाप और the referral of the results of investigations and of suspected criminals to the courts.
विधि प्रवर्तन, to varying डिग्री at अलग स्तर of सरकारी और in अलग एजेंसियों, is भी commonly चार्ज साथ the जिम्मेदारियों of deterring criminal activity and of preventing the successful commission of crimes in progress ; the service and enforcement of warrants, writs and other orders of the courts.
Law enforcement agencies are also involved in providing पहला जवाब to emergencies और अन्य खतरे to पब्लिक सुरक्षा ; the सुरक्षा of निश्चित पब्लिक सुविधाएं और अवसंरचना ; the मेंटेनेंस of पब्लिक अनुक्रम ; the सुरक्षा of पब्लिक officials ; और the आपरेशन of कुछ correctional सुविधाएं ( usually at the local level ).

Galileo Galilei ( ; 15 February 1564 – 8 जनवरी 1642 ), थी an इतालवी physicist, गणितज्ञ, astronomer, और पारस जो निभाई a major role in the Scientific Revolution.
His उपलब्धियाँ शामिल सुधार to the दूरदर्शी और consequent खगोलीय observations और support for Copernicanism.
Galileo has been called the `` father of आधुनिक observational खगोलशास्त्र ``, the `` पिता of आधुनिक भौतिकी ``, the `` पिता of विज्ञान '', और `` the Father of Modern Science ''.
His contributions to observational खगोलशास्त्र शामिल the telescopic पुष्टि of the phases of शुक्र, the डिस्कवरी of the चार largest satellites of बृहस्पति ( नामित the galilean moons in उसके इज्ज़त ), and the observation and analysis of sunspots.
Galileo also worked in applied विज्ञान और प्रौद्योगिकी, inventing an improved सैन्य कम्पास और अन्य यंत्र.
Galileo 's championing of heliocentrism was विवादास्पद भीतर उसके आजीवन, जब सबसे subscribed to either geocentrism or the Tychonic system.
He met with opposition इससे खगोलशास्त्रियों, जो doubted heliocentrism due to the absence of an observed stellar parallax.
The matter was investigated by the रोमन inquisition in 1615, और वे concluded कि it could be समर्थित as only a possibility, not an established fact.
Galileo later defended his views in संवाद concerning the दो मुख्य संसार प्रणालियों, जिससे appeared to आक्रमण पोप शहरी viii और यूँ alienated him and the Jesuits, who had both supported Galileo up until this point.
He was tried by the inquisition, मिला `` ओजस्वी suspect of heresy '', मजबूर to recant, और खर्च the rest of his life under house arrest.
It was जबकि गैलीलियो थी अंतर्गत हाउस गिरफ़्तार कि he लिखा एक of उसके finest works, दो नई sciences, in जिससे he summarised the work he had done some forty years earlier, on the two sciences now called kinematics and strength of materials.

An OLED ( organic light-emitting diode ) is a light-emitting डायोड ( led ) in जिससे the emissive electroluminescent परत is a फिल्मी of सशुल्क यौगिक जिससे emits लाइट in response to an electric current.
This परत of सशुल्क सेमीकंडक्टर is situated between two electrodes.
Generally, at तनिक एक of ये electrodes is transparent.
OLEDs are used to create digital प्रदर्शक in डिवाइस ऐसे as टेलीविज़न screens, computer monitors, portable systems such as mobile phones, handheld games consoles and PDAs.
A major area of research is the development of श्वेत oled डिवाइस लिये उपयोग in solid-state lighting अनुप्रयोग.
वहीँ हैं दो प्रमुख परिवारों of oleds : those based on small molecules and those employing polymers.
Adding mobile ions to an OLED creates a light-emitting electrochemical कोशिका or लैक, जिससे रै a थोड़ा अलग विधि of operation.
oled प्रदर्शक can उपयोग either passive-matrix ( pmoled ) or active-matrix addressing schemes.
Active-matrix OLEDs ( AMOLED ) require a thin-film transistor backplane to switch each individual पिक्सेल on or बंद, लकिन allow लिये उच्चतर रेज़ोल्यूशन और larger प्रदर्शक आकार.
an oled प्रदर्शक works बगैर a backlight.
Thus, it can प्रदर्शक गहन ब्लैक स्तर और can be thinner और हल्का than a द्रव crystal display ( LCD ).
In low ambient light conditions such as a अंधेरा रूम an oled स्क्रीन can achieve a उच्चतर कंट्रास्ट अनुपात than an एलसीडी, whether the LCD uses cold cathode fluorescent lamps or LED backlight.

A pasty (, ), ( sometimes ज्ञात in ब्रिटेन as a cornish pasty, और in the संयुक्त राज्य as a pastie or अंग्रेजों pasty ) is a baked pastry, a traditional variety of which is particularly associated with Cornwall, the westernmost county in England.

The ( ortho- ) सहानुभूतिपूर्ण बेचैन प्रणाली ( sns ) is एक of तीन प्रमुख भाग of the autonomic बेचैन system : the others being the enteric and parasympathetic systems.

Secure डिजिटल or ( sd ) is a non-volatile मेमोरी कार्ड स्वरूप लिये उपयोग in पोर्टेबल डिवाइस, ऐसे as मोबाईल फोन, digital cameras, GPS navigation devices, and tablet computers.
The Secure Digital standard is कायम by the sd कार्ड संघ ( SDA ).
SD technologies have महरूम implemented in अधिक than 400 ब्रांड्स आरपार दर्जनों of उत्पाद categories and more than 8,000 models.
The Secure Digital format includes four card परिवारों उपलब्धियाँ in तीन अलग रूप factors.
The four families are the original Standard-Capacity ( SDSC ), the High-Capacity ( sdhc ), the extended-capacity ( sdxc ), और the sdio, जिससे combines input/output कृत्यों with data storage.
The three form factors are the असली आकार, the `` मिनी '' आकार, और the `` सूक्ष्म '' आकार ( see illustration ).
There are many combinations of रूप कारकों और यंत्र परिवारों.
electrically passive adapters allow the उपयोग of a छोटी कार्ड in a मेजबान यंत्र built to hold a larger card.

A नए कार्ड may प्रस्ताव वृहद क्षमता than the host device can handle.
A newer card may use a file प्रणाली the मेजबान यंत्र can नहीं navigate.
Use of an sdio कार्ड requires the मेजबान यंत्र be designed for the input/output functions the card provides.

Vitamin D is a group of fat-soluble secosteroids जिम्मेदार लिये intestinal अवशोषण of कैल्सियम और फास्फेट.
In humans, the most महत्वपूर्ण सम्बन्धित यौगिकों of विटामिन d हैं विटामिन D2 and vitamin D3.
Cholecalciferol ( vitamin D3 ) and ergocalciferol ( विटामिन d2 ) हैं अद्वितीय as वे constitute कया we जान as विटामिन d और can be ingested इससे the आहार and/or पूरक.
the देह can भी synthesize विटामिन d ( इससे कोलेस्ट्रॉल ) when sun exposure is adequate ( hence its nickname, the `` sunshine vitamin '' ).
Although विटामिन d is commonly पुकारा a विटामिन, it is नहीं दरअसल an अनिवार्य dietary विटामिन in the strict sense, as it can be synthesized in adequate amounts by most mammals exposed to sunlight.
( Cats and dogs can not synthesize विटामिन d efficiently और जरूर प्राप्त it in उनके diet. )
An organic रासायनिक यौगिक ( or सम्बन्धित नियत of यौगिकों ) is तभी scientifically पुकारा a विटामिन जब it can नहीं be synthesized in sufficient quantities by an organism, and must be obtained from their diet.
However, as with other compounds commonly पुकारा विटामिन, विटामिन d थी खोजा in an प्रयत्न to ढूँढें the dietary पदार्थ कि थी lacking in a बीमारी, namely, rickets, the childhood form of osteomalacia.
Additionally, like other compounds called vitamins, in the विकसित संसार विटामिन d is added to स्टेपल भोजन, ऐसे as मिल्क, to avoid बीमारी due to कमियां.
Measures of serum levels reflect endogenous synthesis from exposure to धूप as खूब as सेवन इससे the आहार, और it is believed कि संश्लेषण may योगदान generally to the मेंटेनेंस of पर्याप्त सीरम एकाग्रता.
The evidence indicates that the संश्लेषण of विटामिन d इससे सूर्य एक्सपोज़र works in a प्रतिक्रिया लूप कि रोकता toxicity लकिन, क्युकी of अनिश्चितता परिचय the कर्कट risk from sunlight, no recommendations are issued by the Institute of Medicine, USA, for the amount of sun exposure required to meet vitamin D requirements.
Accordingly, the Dietary Reference Intakes for विटामिन d assume कि no संश्लेषण occurs और कि सब of a व्यक्ति 's विटामिन d is इससे उनके diet, although that will rarely occur in practice.
In the liver vitamin D is converted to calcidiol, जिससे is भी ज्ञात as calcifediol ( इन ), 25-hydroxycholecalciferol, or 25-hydroxyvitamin D—abbreviated 25 ( OH ) D ; and which is the specific vitamin D metabolite that is measured in serum to determine a person 's vitamin D status.
Part of the calcidiol is converted by the kidneys to calcitriol, the biologically active form of विटामिन D. calcitriol circulates as a हार्मोन in the रक्त, regulating the विशेषज्ञता of कैल्सियम और फास्फेट in the bloodstream and promoting the healthy growth and remodeling of bone.
calcidiol is भी परिवर्तित to calcitriol बाहर of the गुर्दे लिये अन्य उद्देश्य, ऐसे as the अप्रसार, differentiation and apoptosis of cells ; calcitriol also affects neuromuscular function and inflammation.
Beyond its use to prevent osteomalacia or rickets, the प्रमाण लिये अन्य स्वास्थ्य प्रभाव of विटामिन d supplementation in the general population is inconsistent.
The best evidence of लाभ is लिये अस्थि स्वास्थ्य और a घटी in mortality in elderly women.
Standard form of the आवधिक तालिका.
The colors represent different श्रेणी of तत्व समझाया नीचे.
The periodic table is a tabular display of the रासायनिक तत्व, व्यवस्थित on the आधार of उनके परमाणु संख्याएँ, इलेक्ट्रॉन configurations, and recurring chemical properties.
Elements हैं प्रस्तुत in अनुक्रम of increasing परमाणु क्रमांक ( number of protons ).
The standard form of table comprises an 18 × 7 ग्रिड or प्रमुख देह of तत्व, positioned ऊपर a smaller double row of elements.
the तालिका can भी be deconstructed into चार आयताकार ब्लॉक : the s-block to the बाएँ, the p-block to the सही, the d-block in the middle, and the f-block below that.
The rows of the table are called periods ; the columns of the s-, d-, और p-blocks हैं पुकारा समूह, साथ कुछ of ये having names ऐसे as the हैलोजन्स or the noble gases.
Since, by definition, a periodic table incorporates recurring trends, any such table can be used to derive संबंध between the गुण of the तत्व और भविष्यवाणी the गुण of नई, yet to be खोजा or synthesized, तत्व.
As a result, a periodic table—whether in the मानक रूप or कुछ अन्य variant—provides a उपयोगी फ्रेमवर्क लिये analyzing रासायनिक बर्ताव, और ऐसे टेबल हैं widely प्रयुक्त in chemistry and other sciences.
Although precursors exist, Dmitri Mendeleev is generally credited साथ the प्रकाशन, in 1869, of the पहला widely recognized periodic table.
He developed उसके तालिका to illustrate आवधिक रुझान in the गुण of the then-known elements.
mendeleev भी पूर्वानुमानित कुछ गुण of then-unknown elements that would be expected to fill gaps in this table.
Most of his predictions were proved correct जब the तत्व in सवाल यहूद subsequently खोजा.
Mendeleev 's periodic table has since been expanded and refined with the discovery or synthesis of further नई तत्व और the विकास of नई सैद्धांतिक मॉडल to बताइये रासायनिक बर्ताव.
All elements from परमाणु संख्याएँ 1 ( हाइड्रोजन ) to 118 ( ununoctium ) have महरूम discovered or synthesized.
the तत्व इससे 1 to 98 ( californium ) have महरूम मिला to मौजूद naturally, हालांकि कुछ हैं मिला तभी in trace amounts and were initially discovered by synthesis in laboratories.
The elements बाद 98 have तभी महरूम synthesized in laboratories.
Production of elements beyond ununoctium is होने धड़ा, साथ the सवाल of कैसा the आवधिक तालिका may need to be modified to accommodate any such additions being a matter of ongoing debate.
numerous सिंथेटिक radionuclides of naturally occurring तत्व have भी महरूम उत्पादित in laboratories.

Bastille Day is the नाम दिए in english-speaking देशों to the फ्रेंच नेशनल दिन, जिससे is मनाये on the 14th of July each year.
In France, it is formally पुकारा la fête nationale ( ; the नेशनल जश्न ) और commonly le quatorze juillet ( ; the fourteenth of July ).
It commemorates the 1790 Fête de la Fédération, held on the first anniversary of the storming of the Bastille on 14 July 1789 ; the वर्षगांठ of the storming of the bastille fortress-prison थी देखी as a प्रतीक of the uprising of the आधुनिक स्वदेश, और of the reconciliation of सब the फ्रेंच अंदर the constitutional monarchy which preceded the First Republic, during the French Revolution.
Festivities and official ceremonies हैं आयोजित सब over France.
The oldest and largest regular military parade in Europe is held on the morning of 14 जुलाई, on the champs-élysées एवेन्यू in पेरिस in सामने of the अध्यक्ष of the गणतंत्र, फ्रेंच officials और विदेशी guests.
The संयुक्त राज्य of अमेरिका ( यूएसए or u.s.A. ), commonly पुकारा the संयुक्त राज्य ( us or u.S. ) or अमेरिका, is a संघीय गणतंत्र consisting of fifty states and a federal district.
The lower forty-eight contiguous states and the संघीय ज़िला of वॉशिंगटन, d.C. हैं in सेंट्रल उत्तर अमेरिका between कनाडा and Mexico.
The state of Alaska is west of Canada and east of Russia आरपार the बेरिंग जलसन्धि, और the राज्य of हवाई is in the mid-north प्रशांत.
The country also has five populated and nine unpopulated territories in the प्रशांत और the caribbean.
At 3.79 million square miles ( 9.83 लाख km2 ) और साथ around 315 लाख लोगों, the संयुक्त राज्य is the third- or fourth-largest देश by total area and the third-largest by both land area and population.
It is one of the संसार 's सबसे ethnically विविध और multicultural राष्ट्र, the उत्पाद of large-scale immigration from many countries.
The geography और जलवायु of the u.S. is भी अत्यधिक विविध, साथ रेगिस्तान, मैदान, वनों, और kyu कि हैं home to a wide variety of species.
Paleoindians migrated from Asia to what is अभी the संयुक्त राज्य मेनलैंड around 15,000 years ago.
बाद 1500, बूढ़ा संसार रोगों introduced by Europeans greatly reduced their populations.
European colonization began around 1600 और आए ज़्यादातर from England.
The United States emerged from thirteen अंग्रेजों colonies located along the Atlantic seaboard.
Disputes between ग्रेट ब्रिटेन और the अमरीकी colonies led to the अमरीकी Revolution.
On July 4, 1776, delegates from the 13 colonies unanimously जारी the घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता, जिससे स्थापित the United States of America.
The American Revolutionary War, जिससे ended साथ the मान्यता of स्वतंत्रता of the संयुक्त राज्य इससे the किंगडम of ग्रेट ब्रिटेन, थी the first successful war of independence against a European colonial empire.
The current Constitution was अपनाया on सितंबर 17, 1787 ; twenty-seven amendments have चूंकि been added to the Constitution.
The first ten amendments, collectively नामित the विधेयक of अधिकारों, यहूद ratified in 1791 और गारंटी अनेक आधारभूत सिविल rights and freedoms.
Driven by the doctrine of manifest नियति, the संयुक्त राज्य embarked on a vigorous विस्तार आरपार North America throughout the 19th century.
This involved displacing native tribes, acquiring new territories, और धीरे admitting नई राज्य.
The American Civil War ended legalized गुलामी in the संयुक्त States.
By the end of the nineteenth सदी, the संयुक्त राज्य विस्तारित into the प्रशांत समंदर, और इसके अर्थव्यवस्था थी the संसार 's largest.
The Spanish–American War and पुष्टि the देश 's औकात as a वैश्विक सैन्य शक्ति.
The United States emerged इससे as a वैश्विक महाशक्ति, the पहला देश साथ नाभिकीय हथियार, and a permanent member of the United Nations Security Council.
The end of the Cold War and the dissolution of the सोवियत संघ बाएँ the संयुक्त राज्य as the sole superpower.
The United States is a developed country and has the world 's largest national economy, with an अनुमानित 2012 जीडीपी of $ 15.6 खरब 19 % of वैश्विक जीडीपी at purchasing-power parity, as of 2011.
The per capita GDP of the U.S. was the world 's sixth-highest as of 2010, हालांकि अमेरिका 's माल असमानता थी भी क्रमित उच्चतम among oecd देशों by the World Bank.
The economy is fueled by an प्रचुरता of प्राकृतिक संसाधन, a well-developed अवसंरचना, और ऊँची उत्पादकता ; और जबकि its economy is considered post-industrial it continues to be one of the world 's largest manufacturers.
The country accounts for 39 % of global military spending, and is a leading economic, political, and cultural force in the संसार, as खूब as a नेता in वैज्ञानिक शोध और technological नवीनता.
The NCAA Men 's Division I Basketball Championship is a single-elimination tournament played each spring in the United States, currently featuring 68 कॉलेज बास्केट टीमों, to determine the नेशनल चैंपियनशिप of the प्रमुख कॉलेज basketball teams.
The tournament, organized by the नेशनल कॉलेजिएट एथलेटिक संघ ( ncaa ), थी निर्मित दौरान 1939 by the नेशनल संघ of Basketball Coaches, and was the idea of Ohio State University coach Harold Olsen.
Played mostly during कूच, it is ज्ञात informally as कूच दीवानगी or the बिग नृत्य, और रै become एक of the सबसे प्रसिद्ध सालाना sporting events in the United States.
The NCAA has credited Bob Walsh of the Seattle आयोजन कमेटी लिये starting the कूच दीवानगी जश्न दौरान 1984.
The tournament teams शामिल champions इससे 31 प्रभाग i सम्मेलनों ( जिससे प्राप्त स्वचालित बोलियों ), और 37 टीमों जिससे are awarded at-large berths.
These `` at-large '' टीमों हैं चुनी by an ncaa चयन कमेटी, as detailed below.
The 64 teams are divided into four regions and व्यवस्थित into a सिंगल विलोपन `` कोष्ठक '', जिससे predetermines, जब a टोली wins a game, which team it will face next.
Each team is `` seeded '', or क्रमित, भीतर its region.
After an initial four games between eight lower-ranked टीमों, the टूर्नामेंट occurs दौरान the कोर्स of तीन सप्ताहांत, at pre-selected न्यूट्रल साइट around the संयुक्त States.
Lower-ranked teams हैं लगाई in the कोष्ठक विरूद्ध उच्चतर क्रमित teams.
Each weekend eliminates three-fourths of the teams, from a round of 64, to a `` Sweet Sixteen '', and लिये the पिछला वीकेंड of the टूर्नामेंट a फाइनल चार ; the फाइनल चार is प्रायः निभाई दौरान the पहला वीकेंड of अप्रैल.
These four teams, one इससे प्रत्येक प्रदेश, तब compete in एक स्थान लिये the national championship.
The tournament has महरूम at तनिक partially televised चूंकि 1969.
Presently, the खेल हैं reported by सीबीएस, tbs, टीएनटी, and truTV by the trade-name NCAA March Madness.
चूंकि 2011, सब खेल are available for viewing nationwide.
As टेलीविज़न कवरेज रै grown, so too has the tournament 's popularity.
Presently, लाखो of अमेरिकी `` भरण आउट a कोष्ठक '', predicting winners of all 67 games.
साथ 11 नेशनल शीर्षक, ucla रै the रिकार्ड लिये the सबसे ncaa मेन 's Division I Basketball Championships ; John Wooden coached UCLA to 10 of its 11 titles.

A नमूना of सिंथेटिक motor oil
Synthetic oil is a lubricant consisting of chemical compounds कि हैं artificially बना ( synthesized ).
Synthetic lubricants can be manufactured using chemically परिवर्धित पेट्रोलियम components बल्कि than पूरे crude आयल, लकिन can भी be synthesized इससे अन्य कच्चा सामग्री.
Synthetic oil is used as a substitute for lubricant refined from पेट्रोलियम जब ऑपरेटिंग in extremes of तापमान, क्युकी, in सामान्य, it provides श्रेष्ठ mechanical और रासायनिक गुण than those found in traditional mineral oils.
Aircraft jet engines, लिये उदाहरण, आवश्यकता the उपयोग of सिंथेटिक oils, whereas aircraft piston engines do not.

francesco albani 's 17th सदी Baptism of Christ is a typical depiction with the sky opening and the Holy Spirit descending as a dove.
The बपतिस्मा of यीशु marks the शुरूआत of his public ministry.
This event is recorded in the canonical gospels of मैथ्यू, चिह्नित और ल्यूक.
John 's gospel does not describe यीशु ' बपतिस्मा, लकिन जॉन the बैपटिस्ट करता गवाही of the अन्य things in.
In the New वसीयत, जॉन the बैपटिस्ट preached the बपतिस्मा of तौबा लिये the remission of पापों ( ), और घोषित खुद a forerunner of he that would baptize `` with the Holy Ghost and with fire '' ( ).
In so doing he was preparing the रास्ता लिये यीशु.
Jesus आए to the जॉर्डन नदी जहाँ he was baptized by John.
The baptismal झाँकी शामिल the आकाश खोलने, a dove-like descent of the पावन स्पिरिट, और a आवाज़ इससे स्वर्ग saying, `` This is my beloved Son, in whom I am well pleased. ''
Most modern विद्वानों दृश्य the फैक्ट कि यीशु थी baptized by जॉन as an ऐतिहासिक इवेंट to which a high degree of certainty can be assigned.
Along with the crucifixion of Jesus most विद्वानों दृश्य it as एक of the दो historically निश्चित तथ्य परिचय उसे, और प्रायः उपयोग it as the starting अंक लिये the study of the historical Jesus.
The baptism is one of the five major milestones in the gospel कथा of the जीवन of यीशु, the अन्य होने the बासीलीक, crucifixion, क़यामत, and Ascension.
Most ईसाई denominations दृश्य the बपतिस्मा of यीशु as an महत्वपूर्ण इवेंट और a basis for the Christian rite of baptism ( see also ).
In पूर्वी christianity, यीशु ' बपतिस्मा is commemorated on 6 जनवरी, the feast of Epiphany.
In the Roman Catholic गिरिजाघर, the anglican नियाज़, the लूथरन चर्च और कुछ अन्य पश्चिमी denominations, it is recalled on a day within the following week, the feast of the baptism of the Lord.
In Roman catholicism, the बपतिस्मा of यीशु is एक of the चमकदार Mysteries sometimes added to the Rosary.
It is a trinitarian feast in the पूर्वी परंपरागत Churches.
Methylcobalamin ( दिखाया ) is a रूप of विटामिन b12.
Physically it resembles the अन्य फ़ॉर्म of विटामिन b12, occurring as अंधेरा रेड crystals कि freely रूप cherry-colored transparent solutions in water.
Vitamin B12, vitamin B12 or vitamin B-12, also called cobalamin, is a water-soluble विटामिन साथ a कुंजी भूमिका in the सामान्य कामकाज of the दिमाग और बेचैन प्रणाली, और for the formation of blood.
it is एक of the eight B vitamins.
It is normally involved in the metabolism of every cell of the इंसान देह, विशेषकर affecting डीएनए संश्लेषण और विनियमन, लकिन भी वसीय एसिड synthesis and energy production.
Neither fungi, plants, nor animals are सक्षम of producing विटामिन b12.
Only bacteria and archaea have the enzymes required for its संश्लेषण, हालांकि अनेक भोजन हैं a प्राकृतिक सोर्स of b12 क्युकी of बैक्टीरियल symbiosis.
The विटामिन is the largest और सबसे structurally जटिल विटामिन और can be produced industrially only through bacterial fermentation-synthesis.
Vitamin B12 consists of a class of chemically सम्बन्धित यौगिकों ( vitamers ), सब of जिससे have विटामिन कार्यकलाप.
it contains the biochemically विरल element cobalt.
Biosynthesis of the मौलिक ढांचा of the विटामिन is संपन्नता तभी by जीवाणु ( जिससे प्रायः उपज hydroxocobalamin ), लकिन परिवर्तन between अलग फ़ॉर्म of the विटामिन can be संपन्नता in the human body.
A common semi-synthetic form of the vitamin, cyanocobalamin, करता नहीं occur in प्रकृति, लकिन is उत्पादित इससे बैक्टीरियल hydroxocobalamin और तब प्रयुक्त in अनेक दवाएँ and supplements, and as a food additive, because of its stability and lower production cost.
In the body it is converted to the इंसान physiological फ़ॉर्म methylcobalamin और adenosylcobalamin, leaving पीछे the साइनाइड, albeit in minimal concentration.
More recently, hydroxocobalamin, methylcobalamin, और adenosylcobalamin can be मिला in अधिक महंगी pharmacological products and food supplements.
The extra utility of ये is फिलहाल debated.
Vitamin B12 was discovered from its relationship to the disease pernicious anemia, which is an autoimmune disease in which parietal कोशिकाएं of the पेट जिम्मेदार लिये secreting मूलभूत फ़ैक्टर हैं नष्ट.
मूलभूत फ़ैक्टर is निर्णायक लिये the सामान्य अवशोषण of b12, so a कमी of मूलभूत फ़ैक्टर, as देखी in घातक anemia, causes a vitamin B12 deficiency.
Many other subtler kinds of विटामिन b12 कमियां और उनके biochemical प्रभाव have चूंकि महरूम elucidated.

Unlike the previous चीख films, वहीँ थी an increased जोर on comedic तत्व और the हिंसा और हॉरर थी घटाया in जवाब to increased public scrutiny about violence in media following the Columbine High School massacre.

The colonial history of the United States covers the history of यूरोपीय settlements इससे the प्रारंभ of colonization of अमेरिका until their incorporation into the United States.
In the late 16th century, England, France, Spain and the नीदरलैंड्स शुभारम्भ प्रमुख colonization कार्यक्रम in पूर्वी North America.
Small early attempts—such as the अंग्रेज़ी खोया उपनिवेश of roanoke —often disappeared ; everywhere the मौत रेट of the first arrivals was very high.
nevertheless कामयाब colonies यहूद established.
European settlers came from a variety of सोशल और धार्मिक समूह.
No aristocrats settled permanently, लकिन a क्रमांक of adventurers, सैनिको, farmers, and tradesmen arrived.
Diversity was an American characteristic as the डच of नई netherland, the swedes और finns of नई स्वीडन, the अंग्रेज़ी quakers of पेन्सिलवेनिया, the अंग्रेज़ी puritans of नई इंग्लैण्ड, the अंग्रेज़ी settlers of Jamestown, and the `` worthy poor '' of Georgia, came to the new continent and built colonies with distinctive social, religious, political and economic styles.
occasionally एक उपनिवेश took कंट्रोल of another ( दौरान युद्धों between उनके European parents ).
Only in Nova Scotia ( अभी भाग of कनाडा ) किया the conquerors निकाल the previous colonists.
Instead they all lived पक्ष by पक्ष in सलाम.
There were no major civil wars among the 13 colonies, and the दो मुख्य हथियारबंद विद्रोहों ( in वर्जिनिया in 1676 और in नई यॉर्क in 1689–91 ) यहूद short-lived असफलताओं.
Wars between the French और the british—the फ्रेंच और भारतीय युद्धों और पिता rale 's युद्ध —were तूल, और शामिल french-support लिये Wabanaki Confederacy attacks on the frontiers.
By 1760 फ़्रांस थी पराजित और the अंग्रेजों जब्त इसके colonies.
The four distinct regions यहूद : नई इंग्लैण्ड, the मध्य colonies, the chesapeake खाड़ी colonies ( Upper South ) and the Lower South.
Some इतिहासकारों add a पांचवां प्रदेश, the frontier, जिससे थी never separately organized.
By the time European settlers arrived around 1600–1650, the majority of the देशी अमेरिकी जीना in the पूर्वी संयुक्त राज्य था महरूम decimated by नई रोगों, introduced to them decades before by explorers and sailors.

Greece ( Romanization of Greek| ), officially the हैलेनिक गणतंत्र ( ' ), is a country in Southeast Europe.
According to the 2011 census, यूनानियों 's जनसांख्यिकी is around 11 million.
Athens is the स्वदेश 's पूंजी और largest नगर, इसके शहरी area also including Piraeus.
Greece is रणनीतिक स्तिथ at the क्रॉसरोड्स of यूरोपीय, एशिया, the मध्य ईस्ट, और अफ़्रीकी, और रै जमीन सीमायें साथ अल्बानियाई, the Republic of Macedonia and Bulgaria to the north, and Turkey to the northeast.
The Aegean Sea lies to the east of मेनलैंड यूनानियों, the आयोनियन समुद्र to the वेस्ट, और the भूमध्यसागरीय Sea to the south.
Greece has the 11th longest coastline in the world at in लंबाई, featuring a विशाल क्रमांक of आइलैंड्स ( लगभग 1,400, of जिससे 227 हैं inhabited ), सहित क्रेट, the dodecanese, the cyclades, और the आयोनियन Islands among others.
Eighty percent of Greece consists of kyu, of जिससे माउंट ओलम्पस is the highest at.
Modern Greece traces इसके जड़ें to the सभ्यता of प्राचीन यूनानियों, generally considered the cradle of Western civilization.
As such, it is the birthplace of democracy, Western philosophy, the Olympic Games, Western literature and historiography, राजनैतिक विज्ञान, प्रमुख वैज्ञानिक और गणितीय सिद्धान्त, and Western drama, including both tragedy and comedy.
This legacy is partly reflected in the सत्रह युनेस्को संसार विरासत साइट स्तिथ in यूनानियों, रैंकिंग it 7th in यूरोपीय और 13th in the world.
The modern Greek state थी स्थापित in 1830, following the यूनानी युद्ध of स्वतंत्रता.
Greece is a founding member of the United Nations, has been a member of कया is अभी the यूरोपीय संघ चूंकि 1981 ( और the eurozone चूंकि 2001 ), और रै महरूम a member of NATO since 1952.
यूनानियों is a विकसित देश साथ an उन्नत, high-income अर्थव्यवस्था और बहुत ऊँची मानकों of living, including the world 's 21st highest quality of life as of 2010.
Greece 's economy is also the largest in the balkans, जहाँ यूनानियों is an महत्वपूर्ण क्षेत्रीय investor.
A prime meridian is a मध्याह्न, i.e. a लकीर of देशांतर, at जिससे देशांतर is पारिभाषित to be 0°.
A प्रधान मध्याह्न और इसके विपरीत in a 360°-system, the 180th meridian ( at 180° longitude ), form a great circle.
This ग्रेट वृत्त divides the गोला, e.g. the Earth, into two hemispheres.
If one uses directions of East and वेस्ट इससे a पारिभाषित प्रधान मध्याह्न, तब वे can be called Eastern Hemisphere and Western Hemisphere.
gerardus मर्केटर in उसके एटलस cosmographicae ( 1595 ) उपयोग a प्रधान मध्याह्न कही बंद to 25°w, गुजर just to the west of Santa Maria Island in the Atlantic.
His 180th meridian runs साथ the जलसन्धि of anián ( Bering Strait )
A prime meridian is ultimately arbitrary, नापसंद an equator, जिससे is संकल्पित by the अक्ष of rotation—and विभिन्न प्रथाओं have महरूम used or advocated in different regions and throughout history.

The Walking Liberty half डालर थी a चांदी 50-cent टुकड़ा or हाफ डालर सिक्का जारी by the संयुक्त राज्य मिंट इससे 1916 to 1947 ; it थी designed by एडाल्फ A. Weinman.
In 1915, the new Mint Director, Robert W. Woolley, came to believe that he थी नहीं तभी अनुमत लकिन जरूरी by विधि to बदलें सिक्का डिजाइन कि था महरूम in उपयोग लिये 25 सालो.
He therefore began the process of replacing the Barber coinage : dimes, quarters और हाफ डॉलर, सब bearing समान डिजाइन by long-time Mint Engraver Charles E. Barber, and first struck in 1892.
Woolley had the Commission of Fine Arts conduct a प्रतियोगिता, as a परिणाम of जिससे weinman थी चयनित to डिज़ाइन the dime और हाफ डालर.
Weinman 's design of Liberty striding towards the सूर्य लिये the हाफ डालर proved मुश्किल to पूर्ण, और राजकोष सचिव विलियम G. mcadoo, जिनकी विभाग included the Mint, considered having Barber create his own design.
Mint officials were successful in getting Weinman 's design into उत्पादन, हालांकि it never struck बहुत खूब, जिससे may have महरूम a फ़ैक्टर in इसके बदलना by the Franklin half dollar beginning in 1948.
Nevertheless, art historian Cornelius vermeule माना the टुकड़ा to be among the सबसे खूबसूरत US coins.
Since 1986, a modification of Weinman 's obverse डिज़ाइन रै महरूम प्रयुक्त लिये the अमरीकी चांदी त्रिभुज.
The Toyota 4Runner is a mid-size खेल यूटिलिटी गाडी ( एसयूवी ) उत्पादित by the जापानी निर्माता टोयोटा और बेची throughout the world from 1984 to present.

इस आलेख सौदे साथ आयुर्विज्ञान as practiced by trained professionals from ancient times to the present.
the प्राचीन उन्होंने था a प्रणाली of आयुर्विज्ञान कि थी बहुत उन्नत लिये इसके time and influenced later medical traditions.
The Egyptians and Babylonians both introduced the अवधारणाओं of निदान, prognosis, और चिकित्सा परिक्षा.
The Greeks went even further, और उन्नत as खूब चिकित्सा ethics.
The Hippocratic Oath, स्टिल लिया by डॉक्टर आज, थी लिखा in यूनानियों in the 5th century BCE.
In the मध्यकालीन era, सर्जिकल practices inherited इससे the प्राचीन मास्टर्स यहूद improved और तब systematized in Rogerius 's The Practice of Surgery.
विश्वविद्यालयों began व्यवस्थित प्रशिक्षण of physicians around the years 1220 in Italy.
दौरान the पुनर्जागरण, समझना of anatomy improved, and the microscope was invented.
The germ theory of disease in the 19th सदी led to cures लिये अनेक संक्रामक रोगों.
Military डॉक्टर उन्नत the विधि of आघात उपचार and surgery.
Public health measures were developed especially in the 19th century as the रैपिड विकास of शहरों जरूरी व्यवस्थित sanitary measures.
उन्नत शोध centers खोली in the जल्दी 20th century, often connected with major hospitals.
The mid-20th सदी थी characterized by नई biological treatments, such as antibiotics.
These advancements, along साथ developments in रसायन, आनुवंशिकी, और lab प्रौद्योगिकी ( such as the x-ray ) led to modern medicine.
Medicine was heavily professionalized in the 20th सदी, और नई करियर opened to women as nurses ( from the 1870s ) and as physicians ( especially after 1970 ).
The 21st सदी is characterized by बहुत उन्नत शोध involving numerous fields of science.
The Hippocratic Corpus, is a संग्रहण of जल्दी चिकित्सा works इससे प्राचीन यूनानियों strongly संबद्ध साथ the प्राचीन Greek physician Hippocrates and his teachings.
पोटैशियम is a रासायनिक तत्व साथ प्रतीक k ( इससे neo-latin kalium ) and atomic number 19.
elemental पोटैशियम is a नरम silvery-white क्षारीय मेटल कि oxidizes rapidly in एयर और is बहुत प्रतिक्रिया साथ जल, generating sufficient heat to ignite the hydrogen emitted in the reaction and burning with a lilac flame.
Because potassium और सोडियम हैं chemically बहुत समान, उनके लवण were not at first differentiated.
The existence of multiple elements in their salts was suspected from 1702, और इस थी सिद्ध in 1807 जब पोटैशियम और सोडियम यहूद individually पृथक इससे अलग लवण by electrolysis.
पोटैशियम in प्रकृति occurs only in ionic salts.
As such, it is found dissolved in seawater ( जिससे is 0.04 % पोटैशियम by वज़न ), और is भाग of many minerals.
Most industrial chemical applications of पोटैशियम employ the अपेक्षाकृत ऊँची घुलनशीलता in जल of पोटैशियम यौगिकों, ऐसे as potassium soaps.
Potassium मेटल रै तभी a few खास अनुप्रयोग, होने replaced in most chemical reactions with sodium metal.
Potassium ions are जरुरी लिये the फलन of सब जीना कोशिकाएं.
पोटैशियम आयन diffusion is a कुंजी यांत्रिकी in तंत्रिका हस्तांतरण, और पोटैशियम depletion in पशु, including humans, results in various cardiac dysfunctions.
Potassium accumulates in संयंत्र कोशिकाएं, और यूँ भैस फल और सब्जियां हैं a good dietary source of it.
Conversely, most plants except विशेषज्ञ halophytes हैं असहिष्णु of नमक, और सोडियम is उपस्थित in उन्हें तभी in low concentration.
This resulted in पोटैशियम पहला होने पृथक इससे potash, the ashes of plants, giving the element its name.
For the वही कारण, भारी क्रॉप उत्पादन rapidly depletes soils of पोटैशियम, and agricultural fertilizers consume 95 % of global potassium chemical production.
the सिंगापुर डालर or डालर ( चिह्न : $ ; कोड : sgd ) is the official currency of Singapore.
It is normally abbreviated with the dollar sign $, or alternatively s $ to फर्क it इससे other dollar -denominated currencies.
It is विभाजित into 100 cents.
The Monetary Authority of Singapore and the Brunei Currency and Monetary Board स्टिल maintain the ऐतिहासिक exchangeability of उनके दो मुद्राएँ, the singaporean डालर और the ब्रुनेई डालर, क्रमशः.
The dollar is accepted as `` प्रथागत टेंडर '' in ब्रुनेई according to the करेंसी interchangeability Agreement.
Likewise, the ब्रुनेई डालर is customarily स्वीकृत in सिंगापुर
James Samuel Coleman ( May 12, 1926 – कूच 25, 1995 ) थी an अमरीकी समाजशास्त्री, theorist और अनुभवजन्य शोधकर्ता, based chiefly at the University of Chicago.
He was elected अध्यक्ष of the अमरीकी समाजशास्त्रीय संघ.
Coleman studied the समाजशास्त्र of शिक्षा, पब्लिक नीति, और थी एक of the earliest users of the term `` social capital ``.
His Foundations of सोशल सिद्धान्त बहकावे समाजशास्त्रीय theory.
His The Adolescent Society ( 1961 ) and `` Coleman Report '' ( Equality of शैक्षणिक अवसर, 1966 ) यहूद दो of the सबसे heavily cited किताबे in शैक्षणिक समाजशास्त्र.
The landmark Coleman Report helped transform educational सिद्धान्त, reshape नेशनल शिक्षा नीतियों, और बहकावे पब्लिक और scholarly राय regarding the भूमिका of schooling in determining equality and productivity in the United States.

A superhero ( sometimes rendered super-hero or super hero ) is a type of stock character possessing `` असाधारण or superhuman शक्तियां '' और समर्पित to protecting the public.
Since the debut of the prototypical सुपरहीरो सुपरमैन in 1938, कहानियां of superheroes—ranging इससे ब्रैड episodic adventures to continuing years-long sagas—have dominated American comic books and crossed over into other media.

A मादा सुपरहीरो is sometimes पुकारा a superheroine ( भी rendered super-heroine or super heroine ).

By most definitions, characters do not strictly require actual superhuman powers to be deemed superheroes, हालांकि शर्तें ऐसे as costumed अपराधों सेनानी or नकाबपोश vigilantes हैं sometimes प्रयुक्त to refer to those ऐसे as बैटमैन और ग्रीन तीर बगैर ऐसे शक्तियां जो share अन्य आम superhero traits.
Such characters were generally referred to as `` रहस्य मेन '' in the so-called सुनहरी आयु of Comic Books to distinguish them from characters with super-powers.
Normally, superheroes use their powers to counter day-to-day crime while also combating खतरे विरूद्ध मानवता by supervillains, उनके दण्ड counterparts.
Often, one of these supervillains होगा be the सुपरहीरो 's archenemy.
As well, some longrunning superheroes, such as Superman, Batman, spider-man और आयरन man प्रत्येक रै a rogues gallery of enemies.
As well, superheroes sometimes will combat such irregular खतरे as एलियंस, magical/ काल्पनिक entities, अमरीकी युद्ध दुश्मनों ऐसे as नात्सीवाद or communism, and godlike or demonic creatures.

North अमेरिका is a महाद्वीप wholly भीतर the उत्तरी गोलार्ध और लगभग wholly within the Western Hemisphere.
it is भी माना a उत्तरी उपमहाद्वीप of the Americas.
It is bordered to the north by the Arctic Ocean, to the east by the Atlantic समंदर, to the वेस्ट और दक्षिण by the प्रशांत समंदर, और to the southeast by दक्षिण अमेरिका और the Caribbean Sea.
North America covers an area of about 24,709,000 वर्गाकार किलोमीटर ( 9,540,000 वर्गाकार मील ), परिचय 4.8 % of the ग्रह 's सतह or परिचय 16.5 % of its land area.
As of July 2008, its population was estimated at nearly 529 लाख लोगों आरपार 23 स्वतंत्र राज्य, representing about 7.5 % of the human population.
North America is the third-largest महाद्वीप in क्षेत्रफल, following एशिया और अफ़्रीकी, और the चौथी in जनसांख्यिकी बाद एशिया, अफ़्रीकी, and Europe.
The first people to live in उत्तर अमेरिका यहूद paleoindians जो began to arrive दौरान the last glacial period by crossing the Bering land bridge.
They differentiated into a number of diverse संस्कृतियों और समुदायों आरपार the महाद्वीप.
The largest and सबसे उन्नत pre-columbian सभ्यताओं in उत्तर अमेरिका यहूद the aztecs in what is now Mexico and the Mayans in Central America.
European colonists began to arrive starting in the 16th और 17th सदियां, wiping आउट विशाल संख्याएँ of the देशी populations और beginning an era of European dominance.

A will or testament is a legal घोषणा by जिससे a व्यक्ति, the testator, names एक or अधिक व्यक्तियों to मैनेज his/her एस्टेट और provides for the transfer of his property at death.
For the devolution of property not disposed of by होगा, देखिए उत्तराधिकार और intestacy.
In the strictest sense, a `` will '' has historically been limited to real property while `` testament '' applies only to dispositions of निजी प्रॉपर्टी ( यूँ giving वृद्धि to the लोकप्रिय शीर्षक of the दस्तावेज़ as `` पिछला होगा और वसीयत '' ), हालांकि इस distinction is seldom observed today.
A will may also create a testamentary विश्वास कि is प्रभावी तभी बाद the मौत of the testator.

Solar energy, रौशन लाइट और ऊष्मा इससे the सूर्य, रै महरूम harnessed by इंसानो चूंकि प्राचीन times using a range of ever-evolving technologies.
Solar energy technologies include solar heating, solar photovoltaics, solar thermal विद्युत, सौर वास्तुकला और कृत्रिम photosynthesis, जिससे can मेक considerable योगदान to solving कुछ of the most urgent energy problems the world now faces.
Solar technologies are broadly characterized as either passive सौर or क्रियाशील सौर depending on the way they capture, convert and distribute solar energy.
Active solar तकनीकों शामिल the उपयोग of photovoltaic panels और सौर थर्मल collectors to harness the energy.
Passive सौर तकनीकों शामिल orienting a भवन to the सूर्य, selecting सामग्री साथ अनुकूल थर्मल द्रव्यमान or light dispersing properties, and designing spaces that naturally circulate air.
In 2011, the International उर्जा एजेंसी कहा कि `` the विकास of सस्ती, inexhaustible और साफ सौर energy technologies will have huge longer-term benefits.
It will increase countries’ energy security through reliance on an स्वदेशी, inexhaustible और ज़्यादातर import-independent संसाधन, बढ़ाएँ स्थिरता, reduce pollution, lower the costs of mitigating climate change, and keep fossil fuel prices lower than otherwise.
ये लाभ are global.
Hence the अतिरिक्त लागत of the प्रोत्साहन लिये जल्दी deployment चाहिए be माना सीखना निवेश ; वे जरूर be बुद्धिमानी spent and need to be widely shared ''.
Sir Thomas More ( ; 7 फ़रवरी 14786 जुलाई 1535 ), ज्ञात to रोमन catholics as संत थामस अधिक चूंकि 1935, थी an अंग्रेज़ी वकील, सोशल पारस, author, statesman, and noted Renaissance humanist.
He was an महत्वपूर्ण पार्षद to हेनरी viii of इंग्लैण्ड और थी रब चांसलर from October 1529 to 16 May 1532.
he थी canonized by पोप पायस xi in 1935 as एक of the जल्दी शहीदो of the schism कि अलग the Church of England from Rome in the 16th century.
In 2000, Pope John Paul II घोषित उसे संरक्षक of कैथोलिक कूटनीतिज्ञों and politicians.
More थी an प्रतिद्वन्दी of the प्रोटोस्टेंट reformation, in particular of मार्टिन Luther and William Tyndale.
However, चूंकि 1980, he is भी commemorated by the गिरिजाघर of England as a reformation martyr.
More coined the word `` utopia `` – a नाम he दिया to the आदर्श और काल्पनिक द्वीप स्वदेश, the राजनैतिक प्रणाली of which he described in Utopia, published in 1516.
he opposed the किंग 's विरह इससे the रोमन कैथोलिक गिरिजाघर और refused to accept उसे as परम् Head of the Church of England, a title which had been given by parliament through the Act of Supremacy of 1534.
He was imprisoned in 1534 for his refusal to take the oath जरूरी by the पहला उत्तराधिकार अधिनियम, क्युकी the अधिनियम disparaged papal प्राधिकार और henry’s marriage to Catherine of Aragon.
In 1535, he was tried for देशद्रोह, convicted on perjured गवाही, और beheaded.
More also helped to originate the phrase `` grasp at लोभी '' to औसत `` शिद्दत trying भी व्यर्थ बाते '', in his Dialogue of Comfort Against Tribulation.
Intellectuals and statesmen आरपार यूरोपीय यहूद दंग by अधिक 's execution.
Erasmus saluted him as one `` whose soul was more pure than कोई हिम, जिनकी प्रतिभाशाली थी ऐसे कि इंग्लैण्ड never था और never again होगा have its like ''.
There was a more controversial side to More 's जीवन, क्युकी he advocated the persecution और निष्पादन of Protestants who refused to recant their faith.
However, the निर्णय of इतिहास रै महरूम largely willing to forgive इस in लाइट of the टाइम्स he जिया in और उसके martyrdom in the Roman Catholic cause.
Two centuries later Jonathan Swift said More was `` the व्यक्ति of the महानतम पुण्य इस किंगडम कभी उत्पादित '', a भावना साथ जिससे सैमुएल जॉनसन सहमत.
इतिहासकार ह्यूज trevor-roper कहा in 1977 कि अधिक थी `` the पहला ग्रेट अंग्रेज जिसको we महसूस कि we जान, the सबसे saintly of humanists, the most human of saints, the universal man of our cool northern renaissance. ''

A modem ( modulator-demodulator ) is a यंत्र कि modulates an एनालॉग वाहक सिग्नल to encode डिजिटल सूचना, और भी demodulates ऐसे a carrier signal to decode the transmitted information.
The लक्ष्य is to उपज a सिग्नल कि can be transmitted easily और decoded to reproduce the original digital data.
Modems can be used over कोई अर्थात् of transmitting एनालॉग सिग्नल, इससे लाइट emitting diodes to radio.
The most familiar example is a voice band modem that turns the digital data of a personal computer into modulated विद्युत सिग्नल in the आवाज़ आवृत्ति दायरा of a टेलीफोन channel.
These signals can be transmitted over टेलीफोन लाइनों और demodulated by another मॉडेम at the receiver side to recover the digital data.
Modems are generally classified by the amount of data they can send in a given unit of time, प्रायः expressed in बिट्स प्रति दूसरी ( bit/s, or bps ), or बाइट्स प्रति दूसरी ( B/s ).
Modems can alternatively be वर्गीकृत by उनके प्रतीक rate, measured in baud.
The baud ईकाई denotes प्रतीकों प्रति दूसरी, or the क्रमांक of times per second the modem sends a new signal.
लिये उदाहरण, the itu v.21 मानक प्रयुक्त ऑडियो आवृत्ति शिफ़्ट keying साथ दो संभावित बारंबारता corresponding to two distinct symbols ( or one bit per symbol ), to carry 300 bits per second using 300 baud.
By contrast, the original ITU V.22 standard, which was able to transmit and receive four distinct प्रतीकों ( दो बिट्स प्रति प्रतीक ), संभाला 1,200 bit/s by sending 600 प्रतीकों प्रति दूसरी ( 600 baud ) using phase शिफ़्ट keying.
The घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता is a बयान अपनाया by the महाद्वीपीय कॉंग्रेस on जुलाई 4, 1776, जिससे घोषित कि the तेरह अमरीकी colonies, then at war with Great Britain, regarded themselves as independent states, and no longer a part of the British Empire.
Instead वे अभी formed a नई nation—the United States of America.
John एडम्स थी a नेता in pushing लिये स्वतंत्रता, जिससे थी unanimously approved on July 2.
A committee had already drafted the औपचारिक घोषणा, to be तैयार when congress voted on independence.
Adams persuaded the committee to चुनें थामस जेफरसन to लिखें the असली ड्राफ्ट of the document, which congress would edit to produce the final version.
The Declaration was ultimately a formal explanation of why Congress had voted on जुलाई 2 to घोषित स्वतंत्रता इससे ग्रेट ब्रिटेन, अधिक than a साल बाद the outbreak of the अमरीकी क्रांतिकारी War.
the नेशनल जन्मदिवस, the स्वतंत्रता दिन is मनाये on July 4, although Adams wanted July 2.
After ratifying the टेक्स्ट on जुलाई 4, कॉंग्रेस जारी the घोषणा of Independence in several forms.
It was initially प्रकाशित as the मुद्रित डनलप broadside कि थी widely distributed and read to the public.
The most famous version of the Declaration, a signed copy that is popularly regarded as the घोषणा of स्वतंत्रता, is प्रदर्शित at the National Archives in Washington, D.C.
Although the wording of the घोषणा थी स्वीकृत on जुलाई 4, the तिथि of its signing was August 2.
The original July 4 United States Declaration of स्वतंत्रता पाण्डुलिपि थी खोया जबकि सब अन्य नक़ल have महरूम निकला इससे this original document.
The sources and interpretation of the घोषणा have महरूम the विषय of much scholarly inquiry.
The Declaration justified the independence of the United States by listing औपनिवेशिक grievances विरूद्ध किंग जार्ज iii, और by asserting निश्चित प्राकृतिक और विधिक अधिकारों, सहित a सही of क्रान्ति.
Having served its original purpose in announcing स्वतंत्रता, the टेक्स्ट of the घोषणा थी initially उपेक्षित बाद the American Revolution.
Since then, it has come to be considered a major statement on इंसान अधिकारों, विशेषकर इसके दूसरी sentence:
We hold ये सच्चाई to be self-evident, कि सब मेन हैं निर्मित बराबर, कि वे हैं endowed by उनके निर्माता साथ निश्चित unalienable अधिकारों, that among these are Life, Liberty and the pursuit of Happiness.
This has been called `` one of the best-known वाक्य in the अंग्रेज़ी भाषा '', containing `` the सबसे potent और consequential शब्द in अमरीकी इतिहास. ''
The passage came to represent a moral मानक to जिससे the संयुक्त राज्य should strive.
This view was notably promoted by Abraham lincoln, जो माना the घोषणा to be the न्यास of उसके राजनैतिक दर्शनशास्त्र, और argued कि the घोषणा is a statement of principles through which the United States Constitution should be interpreted.
It has inspired work for the rights of अधिकारहीन लोगों throughout the संसार.
The अर्थव्यवस्था of ग्रीनलैंड can be characterized as छोटी, मिश्रित and vulnerable.
The present economy consists of a big public sector and comprehensive विदेशी व्यापार, जिससे रै resulted in an अर्थव्यवस्था साथ अवधि of दमदार विकास, considerable महंगाई, बेरोजगारी problems and extreme dependence on capital inflow from Denmark and use of outside, mainly Danish, skilled labor.
GDP per capita is similar to the average European economies but the अर्थव्यवस्था is critically निर्भर upon substantial support इससे the डैनिश सरकारी, जिससे आपूर्तियाँ परिचय हाफ the revenues of the घर नियम सरकारी who in turn employ about 8,000 Greenlanders out of a labor force of 40,156 ( Jan. 2012 ).
Unemployment nonetheless remains high, with the बाकी of the अर्थव्यवस्था निर्भर upon माँग लिये निर्यात of झींगा और मछली.
Hydrogen is a रासायनिक तत्व साथ प्रतीक h और परमाणु number 1.
With an atomic weight of ( for hydrogen-1 ), हाइड्रोजन is the lightest तत्व और इसके monatomic रूप ( h1 ) is the सबसे abundant रासायनिक पदार्थ, constituting roughly 75 % of the Universe 's baryonic mass.
Non- remnant stars are मुख्यतः रचित of हाइड्रोजन in इसके प्लाज्मा state.
At standard temperature and pressure, hydrogen is a colorless, गंधहीन, tasteless, non-toxic, nonmetallic, अत्यधिक combustible diatomic गैस साथ the आणविक formula H2.
Most of the hydrogen on Earth is in अणुओं ऐसे as जल और सशुल्क यौगिकों क्युकी हाइड्रोजन readily forms covalent compounds with most non-metallic elements.
हाइड्रोजन plays a विशेषकर महत्वपूर्ण भूमिका in acid-base रसायन साथ अनेक प्रतिक्रियाएँ exchanging protons between soluble molecules.
In ionic compounds, it can take a negative charge ( an anion ज्ञात as a हाइड्राइड और लिखा as h− ), or as a positively charged species H+.
The latter cation is written as though composed of a bare प्रोटॉन, लकिन in वास्तविकता, हाइड्रोजन cations in ionic यौगिकों सदा occur as more complex species.
The most common isotope of hydrogen is protium ( name rarely used, symbol 1h ) साथ a सिंगल प्रोटॉन और no neutrons.
As the simplest atom known, the हाइड्रोजन अणु रै महरूम of सैद्धांतिक उपयोग.
For example, as the तभी न्यूट्रल अणु साथ an analytic समाधान to the श्रोडिंगर समीकरण, the पढ़ाई of the energetics और संबंध of the हाइड्रोजन अणु played a key role in the development of quantum mechanics.
Hydrogen gas was first artificially produced in the जल्दी 16th सदी, via the mixing of धातुओं with acids.
in 1766–81, हेनरी कैवेंडिश थी the पहला to recognize कि हाइड्रोजन गैस थी a अलहदा पदार्थ, और कि it produces जल जब burned, a प्रॉपर्टी which later gave it its name : in Greek, hydrogen means `` water-former ''.
Industrial उत्पादन is मुख्यतः इससे the भाप reforming of प्राकृतिक गैस, और कम प्रायः इससे अधिक energy-intensive हाइड्रोजन उत्पादन methods like the electrolysis of water.
सबसे हाइड्रोजन is employed निकट इसके उत्पादन साईट, साथ the दो largest उपयोग होने चट्टान ईंधन प्रसंस्करण ( e.g., hydrocracking ) and ammonia production, mostly for the fertilizer market.
Hydrogen is a concern in metallurgy as it can embrittle अनेक धातुओं, complicating the डिज़ाइन of pipelines और भंडार टैंक.

in छायाचित्र, bracketing is the सामान्य तकनीक of taking several shots of the same subject using different camera settings.
Bracketing is useful and प्रायः अनुशंसित in परिस्थितियों कि मेक it मुश्किल to obtain a संतोषजनक चित्र साथ a सिंगल शॉट, विशेषकर जब a छोटी विभिन्नता in exposure parameters has a comparatively large effect on the resulting image.
Autobracketing is automatic bracketing by using a सेटिंग on the कैमरा to लो अनेक bracketed गोलियाँ ( in कंट्रास्ट to the फ़ोटोग्राफ़र altering the settings by hand between each shot ).
Given the time it takes to accomplish multiple shots, it is typically, लकिन नहीं सदा, प्रयुक्त लिये स्थिर विषय.
Insulated glazing ( IG ), more commonly known as double glazing ( or double-pane, और increasingly ट्रिपल glazing/pane ) हैं दोगुना or ट्रिपल कांच खिड़की panes अलग by an एयर or अन्य गैस भर स्पेस to reduce ऊष्मा ट्रांसफ़र across a part of the building envelope.
insulated कांच इकाई हैं manufactured साथ कांच in दायरा of मोटाई from 3 mm to 10 mm or more in special applications.
Laminated or tempered कांच may भी be प्रयुक्त as भाग of the निर्माण.
सबसे इकाई हैं manufactured साथ the वही मोटाई of कांच प्रयुक्त on दोनो panes लकिन खास अनुप्रयोग ऐसे as ध्वनिक क्षीणन or security may require wide ranges of thicknesses to be incorporated in the same unit.
A sectioned आरेख of a फिक्स्ड insulated चमकीले ईकाई ( igu ), indicating the numbering convention used in this article.
सतह # 1 is facing बाहर, सतह # 2 is the अंदर सतह of the exterior फलक, सतह # 3 is the outside surface of the interior pane, and Surface # 4 is the inside surface of interior pane.
The window frame is labelled # 5, a spacer is indicated as # 6, seals हैं दिखाया in रेड ( # 7 ), the आतंरिक खुलासा is on the सही हाथ पक्ष ( # 8 ) and the exterior windowsill on the left ( # 9 )
To reduce shear effects on the sealed ईकाई ( a प्रमुख कारण of असामयिक विफलता ), निर्माताओं उपयोग a नियम of अंगूठा कि permits a अंतर of 1 mm between the thickness of the panes of glass used in the unit and still maintain the warranty for the unit.
For example, a unit may be ordered साथ a 4 mm फलक on the exterior और a 3 mm फलक on the interior.
These विसंगतियाँ हैं अनुमत लिये architectural और cost reasons.
Other combinations can be निर्दिष्ट और उत्पादित लकिन the निर्माता may आरक्षित the सही to सीमा the पद of the वारंटी or refuse to warranty the unit altogether.
For ease of description the surfaces of a double paned ईकाई हैं नामित according to the following सम्मेलन : सतह # 1 ( facing बाहर ), सतह # 2 ( अंदर of बाहर फलक ), सतह # 3 ( बाहर of अंदर फलक ) and Surface # 4 ( inside surface of inside pane ).
Applying the corresponding नामकरण लिये ट्रिपल paned इकाई परिणाम in सतहों # 1 through # 6.

Selenium is a रासायनिक तत्व साथ प्रतीक se और परमाणु number 34.
It is a nonmetal with properties that are इंटरमीडिएट between those of इसके आवधिक तालिका column-adjacent chalcogen तत्व sulfur and tellurium.
It rarely occurs in इसके elemental राज्य in प्रकृति, or as pure ore compounds.
Selenium ( Greek σελήνη selene अर्थ `` चंद्रमा '' ) थी खोजा in 1817 by jöns याक़ूब berzelius, जो विख्यात the समानता of the नई तत्व to the previously-known tellurium ( named for the Earth ).
Selenium is found impurely in metal sulfide ores, जहाँ it partially replaces the गंधक.
Commercially, selenium is उत्पादित as a byproduct in the शोधन of ये ores, सबसे प्रायः दौरान तांबे उत्पादन.
Minerals that are pure selenide or selenate यौगिकों हैं ज्ञात, but are rare.
The chief commercial uses for selenium आज हैं in glassmaking और in pigments.
Selenium is a सेमीकंडक्टर और is प्रयुक्त in photocells.
Uses in electronics, once महत्वपूर्ण, have महरूम ज़्यादातर supplanted by silicon semiconductor devices.
Selenium continues to be प्रयुक्त in a few प्रकार of dc शक्ति surge protectors and one type of fluorescent quantum dot.
Selenium salts are toxic in large amounts, लकिन ट्रेस amounts हैं जरुरी लिये सेल्यूलर फलन in अनेक जीवों, सहित all animals.
Selenium is a component of the एंटीऑक्सीडेंट एंजाइमों glutathione peroxidase और thioredoxin reductase ( जिससे indirectly reduce निश्चित oxidized molecules in animals and some plants ).
It is also found in तीन deiodinase एंजाइमों, जिससे बदलें एक थायराइड hormone to another.
Selenium requirements in plants differ by प्रजाति, साथ कुछ पौधे requiring अपेक्षाकृत विशाल amounts, और अन्य apparently requiring none.

Visualization of fragmentation और तब of defragmentation
In the maintenance of file systems, defragmentation is a प्रक्रम कि reduces the amount of fragmentation.
It does इस by physically आयोजन the सामग्री of the द्रव्यमान भंडार यंत्र प्रयुक्त to स्टोर फाइलें into the smallest number of contiguous regions ( fragments ).
It also attempts to create larger regions of free स्पेस using compaction to impede the वापसी of fragmentation.
Some defragmentation utilities try to रखना छोटी फाइलें भीतर a सिंगल निर्देशिका साथ, as वे हैं प्रायः accessed in sequence.
defragmentation is लाभदायक और प्रासंगिक to संचिका प्रणालियों on electromechanical disk drives.
The movement of the hard drive 's read/write heads over अलग क्षेत्रों of the डिस्क जब accessing fragmented फाइलें is धीमा, compared to accessing the entire contents of a non-fragmented file sequentially without moving the read/write heads to seek other fragments.
A service-level agreement ( SLA ) is a भाग of a सेवा अनुबंध जहाँ a सेवा is formally पारिभाषित.
In practice, the term SLA is sometimes used to refer to the contracted डिलीवरी समय ( of the सेवा or performance ).
As an example, अंतरजाल सेवा प्रदाताओं होगा commonly शामिल सेवा स्तर समझौतों भीतर the शर्तें of उनके contracts with customers to define the level ( s ) of service being sold in plain language terms.
In this case the SLA will typically have a technical definition in terms of mean time between असफलताओं ( mtbf ), औसत समय to मरम्मत or औसत समय to रिकवरी ( mttr ) ; विभिन्न आंकड़ा दरों ; throughput ; जिटर ; or समान measurable details.

Utilization management is the मूल्यांकन of the appropriateness, चिकित्सा need और दक्षता of स्वास्थ्य परवाह सेवाएं प्रक्रियाओं और सुविधाएं according to स्थापित मापदण्ड or दिशानिर्देश और अंतर्गत the provisions of an applicable health benefits plan.
typically it शामिल नई क्रियाएँ or decisions based upon the analysis of a case.
Utilization management describes proactive प्रक्रियाओं, सहित निर्वहन नियोजन, संयुक्त planning, pre-certification and clinical case appeals.
It भी कवर proactive प्रक्रियाओं, ऐसे as संयुक्त नैदानिक समीक्षाएँ और पीर समीक्षाएँ, as well as appeals introduced by the provider, payer or patient.
As pre-certification and संयुक्त पुनर्विलोकन of मामले grew, utilization प्रबन्धन spun आउट of utilization review.
While not synonymous, health परवाह पेशेवर tend to उपयोग the शर्तें as interchangeable.
The difference is utilization management is and intends to मैनेज स्वास्थ्य परवाह मामले efficiently और लागत effectively पहले और दौरान health care administration.
Utilization review is more considering whether स्वास्थ्य परवाह थी appropriately लागू बाद it थी administered.

Skin is the नरम बाहरी covering of vertebrates.
Other animal coverings such as the arthropod exoskeleton have अलग developmental उत्पत्ति, ढांचा और रासायनिक composition.
The adjective cutaneous अर्थात् `` of the स्किन '' ( इससे लैटिन cutis, skin ).
In mammals, the skin is the largest organ of the integumentary system made up of multiple layers of ectodermal tissue, and गार्ड the underlying मांसपेशियां, हड्डियों, ligaments और आतंरिक अंगों.

All mammals have कुछ बाल on उनके स्किन, भी समुद्री स्तनधारियों which appear to be hairless.
The skin interfaces with the पर्यावरण और is the पहला लकीर of defense from external factors.
For उदाहरण, the स्किन plays a कुंजी भूमिका in protecting the देह against pathogens and excessive water loss.
Its other functions are insulation, तापमान विनियमन, सनसनी, और the उत्पादन of vitamin D folates.

This is sometimes discoloured और depigmented.

In humans for example, the skin located under the आँखें और around the eyelids is the thinnest स्किन in the देह at 0.5 mm मोटा, और is one of the first areas to show signs of aging such as `` crows feet '' and wrinkles.
The skin on the हथेलियां और the सोल्स of the फीट is 4 mm thick and the thickest skin in the body.
फर is घना hair.

On some animals, the स्किन is बहुत मुश्किल और मोटा, और can be processed to बनाएँ चमड़े.
Reptiles and मछली have मुश्किल सुरक्षात्मक तराजू on उनके स्किन लिये सुरक्षा, और पक्षियों have hard feathers, all made of tough β- keratins.
