A twelve-step program is a set of guiding principles ( accepted by members as 'spiritual सिद्धान्त, ' आधारित on the स्वीकृत साहित्य ) outlining a कोर्स of कार्रवाई लिये रिकवरी इससे, मजबूरी, or अन्य behavioral problems.
originally प्रस्तावित by alcoholics बेनाम ( aa ) as a विधि of रिकवरी इससे alcoholism, the बारह कदम यहूद पहला प्रकाशित in the किताब alcoholics Anonymous : The Story of How More Than One Hundred Men Have Recovered from Alcoholism in 1939.
The method was then adapted and became the न्यास of अन्य twelve-step programs.
As summarized by the अमरीकी मनोवैज्ञानिक संघ, the process involves the following:
admitting कि एक can नहीं कंट्रोल एक 's addiction or compulsion ;
recognizing a उच्चतर शक्ति कि can दे शक्ति ;
examining past errors with the सहायता of a प्रायोजक ( अनुभवी सदस्य ) ;
making amends लिये ये त्रुटियाँ ;
सीखना to सजीव a new life with a new code of behavior ;
helping अन्य जो suffer इससे the वही व्यसनों or compulsions.

following the outbreak of संसार युद्ध i in 1914, the जर्मनी फौज खोली the पश्चिमी सामने by पहला invading Luxembourg and Belgium, then gaining military control of important industrial regions in France.
The tide of the advance was dramatically turned साथ the बैटल of the Marne.
Following the race to the sea, both sides dug in साथ a meandering लकीर of fortified trenches, stretching from the North Sea to the Swiss frontier with France.
This line remained essentially अपरिवर्तित लिये सबसे of the war.
Between 1915 and 1917 वहीँ यहूद अनेक प्रमुख offensives साथ इस सामने.
The attacks employed विशाल तोपखाने bombardments और massed infantry advances.
However, a combination of entrenchments, machine gun nests, barbed तार, और तोपखाने repeatedly inflicted कठोर हताहत on the हमलावर और counterattacking defenders.
As a परिणाम, no significant advances were made.
Among the most costly of these offensives were the Battle of Verdun with a combined [ estimated ] 700,000 मुर्दे, the बैटल of the somme साथ अधिक than [ an अनुमानित ] लाख हताहत, और the बैटल of passchendaele साथ roughly [ an estimated ] 600,000 casualties.
In an effort to ब्रेक the deadlock, इस सामने देखी the परिचय of नई सैन्य technology, including poison gas, aircraft and tanks.
But it was only after the अपनाना of improved tactics कि कुछ उपाधि of गतिशीलता थी लौटी.
The German Spring Offensive of 1918 was made संभावित by the सन्धि of brest-litovsk कि चिह्नित the समाप्त of the विरोध on the Eastern Front.
Using the recently-introduced infiltration tactics, the German सेना उन्नत nearly to the वेस्ट, जिससे चिह्नित the deepest अग्रिम by either पक्ष चूंकि 1914 और बहुत nearly succeeded in forcing a breakthrough.
In spite of the generally stagnant प्रकृति of इस सामने, इस थिएटर होता prove निर्णायक.
The inexorable advance of the Allied armies during the second half of 1918 persuaded the जर्मनी कमांडरों कि शिकस्त थी अपरिहार्य, और the सरकारी थी मजबूर to मुकदमा लिये शर्तें of an armistice.
The terms of peace were सहमत upon साथ the हस्ताक्षर of the सन्धि of versailles in 1919.

It can कारण अनेक अंग dysfunction सिंड्रोम ( formerly known as multiple organ failure ) and death.

Multi-pitch climbing is the ascent of चढ़ाई रूट साथ एक or अधिक stops at a belay station.
Each section of वास्तविक चढ़ाई between stops at the belay stations is called a pitch.
The leader ascends the pitch, placing gear and stopping to लंगर themselves to the belay स्टेशन.
The कारण लिये the stops can be संकल्पित by चुनाव, convention or necessity.
For example:
The रस्सी is too छोटी to do the संपूर्ण रूट in one pitch ( necessity ).
the नेता रै चलाएं आउट of सुरक्षात्मक gear ( necessity ).
There is a सुविधाजनक protectable कगार, or फिक्स्ड bolts लगाई by पिछला चढना, at the location for a belay station ( convention ).
The leader chooses to rest or एक्सचेंज लीड पहले the अगला खण्ड of the climb ( choice ).
The general purpose of ये stops is to allow the दूसरी to ascend to the पाइंट of the सीसे climber जबकि collecting the protective gear from the route in the course of the lead climber 's ascent.
At the belay station, the सुरक्षात्मक गियर is एकत्रित, संभवतः exchanged to a नई नेता, and the leader of the next pitch ascends the route.

The specific role that a player takes on the फ़ील्ड is पुकारा उनके स्थिति.
Under the modern rules of American football, teams हैं अनुमत असीमित subsititutions, कि is टीमों may बदलें any number of players after any play.
This has resulted in the विकास of तीन `` platoons '' of खिलाड़ी, the ठोकर ( the टोली साथ the बॉल, जो is trying to स्कोर ), the रक्षा ( the टोली trying to prevent the other team from scoring, and to take the ball from them ), and the special teams ( who play in kicking situations ).

The Controlled Substances Act ( CSA ) was enacted into law by the Congress of the संयुक्त राज्य as शीर्षक ii of the व्यापक ड्रग गाली रोकथाम and Control Act of 1970.
The CSA is the federal U.S. drug नीति अंतर्गत जिससे the manufacture, importation, कब्ज़ा, उपयोग और वितरण of certain substances is regulated.
The Act also परोसा as the नेशनल implementing विधान लिये the सिंगल सम्मेलन on Narcotic Drugs.
the विधान निर्मित पाँच schedules ( classifications ), साथ varying qualifications for a substance to be included in each.
Two federal agencies, the Drug Enforcement Administration और the खाना और ड्रग प्रशासन, determine जिससे substances हैं added to or removed इससे the विभिन्न schedules, हालांकि the statute passed by कॉंग्रेस निर्मित the आरंभिक लिस्टिंग, और कॉंग्रेस रै sometimes अनुसूचित अन्य substances through विधान ऐसे as the hillory J. farias और सामन्था reid date-rape रोकथाम अधिनियम of 2000, जिससे लगाई गामा hydroxybutyrate in Schedule I. Classification decisions are required to be made on criteria including potential for abuse ( an undefined term ), currently accepted medical use in treatment in the United States, and international treaties.

The at sign @ is also commonly called the at symbol, ampersat, apetail or वाणिज्यिक at in english—and कम commonly a चौड़ी दायरा of अन्य शर्तें.
The fact that there is no single word in English for the प्रतीक रै prompted कुछ लेखक to उपयोग the फ्रेंच arobase or स्पेनी और पुर्तगाली arroba—or to सिक्का नई शब्द ऐसे as asperand, ampersat—but none of these has achieved wide currency.
Originally an accounting and commercial invoice abbreviation meaning `` at the rate of '' ( e.g. 7 विजेट @ $ 2 = $ 14 ), it थी नहीं शामिल on the कुंजीपटल of the earliest commercially कामयाब typewriters, लकिन थी on at तनिक एक 1889 मॉडल और the बहुत कामयाब Underwood models from the `` Underwood No. 5 '' in 1900 onward.
It is now universally शामिल on कंप्यूटर keyboards.
In recent years, its meaning has grown to include the sense of being `` located at, '' `` and, '' or `` directed at '', विशेषकर in ईमेल पता और सोशल मीडिया, विशेषकर ट्विटर.
The mark is एनकोडेड at.

skeletal मांसपेशियां होमो sapiens
इस is a तालिका of मांसपेशियां of the human anatomy.
There are approximately 642 skeletal muscles within the ठेठ इंसान, और लगभग प्रत्येक मांसपेशी constitutes एक भाग of a जोड़ी of एकसमान द्विपक्षीय मांसपेशियां, मिला on दोनो पहलू, resulting in लगभग 320 pairs of मांसपेशियां, as प्रस्तुत in this article.

The muscles of the human body can be categorized into a क्रमांक of समूह जिससे शामिल मांसपेशियां relating to the सिर और गर्दन, मांसपेशियां of the धड़ or ट्रंक, मांसपेशियां of the अपर limbs, and muscles of the lower limbs.

mechanical मरम्मत
Maintenance, repair, and operations ( MRO ) or maintenance, repair, और overhaul involves फिक्सिंग कोई sort of mechanical, plumbing or विद्युत यंत्र चाहिए it become आउट of अनुक्रम or broken ( known as repair, unscheduled or casualty maintenance ).
It also includes performing दिनचर्या क्रियाएँ जिससे रखना the यंत्र in working अनुक्रम ( ज्ञात as अनुसूचित maintenance ) or prevent trouble from arising ( preventive maintenance ).
MRO may be defined as, `` All actions which have the objective of retaining or restoring an मद in or to a राज्य in जिससे it can perform इसके जरूरी function.
The actions include the combination of all तकनीकी और सम्बन्धित प्रशासनिक, managerial, और पर्यवेक्षण actions. ''
MRO operations can be categorised by whether the product remains the property of the customer, i.e. a service is being offered, or whether the उत्पाद is खरीदा by the reprocessing संगठन और बेची to कोई ग्राहक wishing to मेक the खरीदें ( Guadette, 2002 ).
In the former case it may be a backshop आपरेशन भीतर a larger संगठन or छोटी आपरेशन.
the पूर्व of ये represents a बंद लूप सप्लाई कड़ी और प्रायः रै the पैमाना of maintenance, repair or of the product.
The latter of the categorisations is an खोलें लूप सप्लाई कड़ी और is typified by refurbishment और remanufacture.
The प्रमुख characteristic of the बंद लूप प्रणाली is कि the माँग लिये a उत्पाद is matched with the supply of a used product.
Neglecting asset write-offs और असाधारण क्रियाएँ the कुल जनसांख्यिकी of the उत्पाद between the ग्राहक और the service provider remains constant.

The electron हस्तांतरण कड़ी in the सूत्रकणिका is the साईट of oxidative phosphorylation in eukaryotes.
The NADH and succinate generated in the साइट्रिक एसिड साईकिल हैं oxidized, providing उर्जा to शक्ति एटीपी synthase.
Photosynthetic इलेक्ट्रॉन हस्तांतरण कड़ी of the thylakoid membrane.
An electron transport chain ( ETC ) couples electron transfer between an electron donor ( such as nadh ) और an इलेक्ट्रॉन acceptor ( ऐसे as o2 ) साथ the ट्रांसफ़र of H+ ions ( protons ) आरपार a झिल्ली.
The resulting electrochemical proton gradient is used to generate रासायनिक उर्जा in the रूप of एडीनोसिन ट्राइफॉस्फेट ( एटीपी ).
Electron transport chains are the cellular mechanisms प्रयुक्त लिये extracting उर्जा इससे धूप in photosynthesis और भी इससे रेडॉक्स प्रतिक्रियाएँ, ऐसे as the oxidation of sugars ( respiration ).
In chloroplasts, लाइट ड्राइव the परिवर्तन of जल to ऑक्सीजन और nadP+ to nadph साथ ट्रांसफ़र of H+ ions across chloroplast membranes.
In mitochondria, it is the परिवर्तन of ऑक्सीजन to जल, nadh to naD+ और succinate to fumarate that are required to generate the proton gradient.
Electron हस्तांतरण जंजीरों हैं प्रमुख साइट of असामयिक इलेक्ट्रॉन leakage to ऑक्सीजन, generating superoxide and potentially resulting in increased oxidative stress.

the ड्रग रै a चौड़ी दायरा of अनुप्रयोग, सहित उपचार of आमवातीय गठिया, restless legs syndrome, motor neurone disease and fibromyalgia.

Tramadol is a weak μ-opioid receptor agonist कि भी induces serotonin रिलीज and inhibits the reuptake of norepinephrine.
Tramadol is metabolized to o-desmethyltramadol, a significantly अधिक potent μ-opioid agonist.
Tramadol and its major metabolite ( s ) are distinguished इससे अन्य अधिक potent opioid agonists by सापेक्ष selectivity लिये μ-opioid receptors.
Bernard Lawrence `` Bernie '' Madoff ( ; born April 29, 1938 ) is an अमरीकी पूर्व stockbroker, निवेश सलाहकार, फाइनेंसर, और श्वेत कॉलर दण्ड.

On December 10, 2008, Madoff 's sons told authorities that their father had confessed to them that the एसेट प्रबन्धन ईकाई of उसके कड़ थी a विशाल पेन्शन योजना, और कोटेड उसे as describing it as `` एक बिग झूठ. ''

The U.S. प्रतिभूति और एक्सचेंज आयोग ( सेक ) था previously conducted investigations into Madoff 's business practices, but did not uncover the massive fraud.

A quasi-judicial body is an entity such as an arbitrator or tribunal board, generally of a public administrative एजेंसी, जिससे रै शक्तियां और प्रक्रियाओं resembling those of a अदालत of विधि or न्यायधीश, और जिससे is obligated to objectively determine तथ्य and draw conclusions from them so as to provide the basis of an official action.
Such actions are able to remedy a situation or impose legal दंड, और may affect the विधिक अधिकारों, कर्तव्य or privileges of विशिष्ट पार्टियों.

Tycho Brahe ( 14 December 154624 October 1601 ), born Tyge Ottesen Brahe, was a Danish nobleman ज्ञात लिये उसके सटीक और व्यापक खगोलीय और ग्रहीय observations.
He was born in Scania, then part of डेनमार्क, अभी भाग of modern-day स्वीडन.
Tycho थी खूब ज्ञात in उसके आजीवन as an astronomer and alchemist.
in उसके de नोवा स्टेला ( on the नई स्टार ) of 1573, he refuted the aristotelian belief in an unchanging celestial realm.
His precise measurements indicated कि `` नई सितारों, '' ( stellae novae, अभी ज्ञात as supernovae ) in particular कि of 1572, lacked the लंबन अपेक्षित in sub-lunar phenomena, और यहूद इसलिए not `` atmospheric '' tailless comets as previously believed, but were above the atmosphere and moon.
Using similar measurements he दिखाया कि धूमकेतुओं यहूद भी नहीं वायुमंडलीय phenomena, as previously विचार, और जरूर pass through the माना `` immutable '' celestial spheres.
As an astronomer, Tycho worked to combine what he saw as the geometrical लाभ of the copernican प्रणाली साथ the philosophical लाभ of the ptolemaic प्रणाली into उसके अपना मॉडल of the ब्रह्मांड, the Tychonic system.
Furthermore, he was the पिछला of the प्रमुख नग्न नजर खगोलशास्त्रियों, working बगैर telescopes for his observations.
Tycho Brahe was granted an estate on the द्वीप of hven और the funding to निर्माण the uraniborg, an जल्दी शोध संस्थान, जहाँ he निर्मित विशाल खगोलीय यंत्र और took अनेक careful माप, and later Stjerneborg, underground, when he discovered that his instruments in the former were not sufficiently steady.
On the island ( on which he demonstrated निरंकुश अक्षर और बर्ताव toward the निवासियों ) he संस्थापित manufactories ऐसे as paper-making to provide सामग्री लिये मुद्रण his results.
After मतभिन्नता साथ the नई डैनिश किंग ईसाई iv in 1597, he थी आमंत्रित by the bohemian किंग और पावन Roman emperor Rudolph II to Prague, where he became the official imperial astronomer.
He निर्मित the नई वेधशाला at Benátky nad Jizerou.
Here, from 1600 until his death in 1601, he was assisted by योहानेस कॅप्लर जो बाद प्रयुक्त tycho 's खगोलीय आंकड़ा to develop कॅप्लर 's laws of planetary motion.
Guro District ( Guro-gu ) is a district of Seoul, South Korea, जिससे थी अलग इससे yeongdeungpo ज़िला on अप्रैल 1, 1980.
Located in the southwestern part of the city, where besides yangcheon ज़िला और geumcheon ज़िला guro ज़िला रै an महत्वपूर्ण स्थिति as a हस्तांतरण कड़ी जिससे contains railroads, जमीन रूट इससे the बाकी of Seoul to the south of the country.
The Gyeongbu and Gyeongin railway lines कनेक्ट सियोल to बुसान और इंचियोन.
In addition, Seoul Metropolitan Subway lines 1, 2, और 7, और प्रमुख राजमार्गों प्रतिच्छेद in Guro District.
The name Guro originates इससे the लेजेंड कि नौ ( ) बूढ़ा मेन ( कोरियाई : ro ) enjoyed आयु in the district.
A digital औद्योगिक जटिल is स्तिथ in guro District.
The Guro Digital Industrial Complex, which played a leading industrial role mainly with textile निर्माण, dressmaking और अन्य labour-intensive उद्योग in 1967, रै महरूम rapidly बदला into an it औद्योगिक complex.
This complex played a pivotal role in the आर्थिक विकास of the दक्षिण कोरियाई 's विकास era, referred to as the `` चमत्कार on the हान नदी ``, और also contributed 10 percent of national export in the 1970s.
Twenty-one percent of the total area of Guro District is a प्रतिबंधित मण्डल to be प्रयुक्त as a greenbelt साथ the तभी arboretum in Seoul.
The zone is changing into a lively district as विशाल labour-intensive कारखानों हैं चलती इससे the क्षेत्रफल और the परिषद is developing what it terms its four zones.
An `` e-government `` system आधारित on इस hosted the अंतरराष्ट्रीय e-participation फ़ोरम on फ़रवरी 7–9, 2007, साथ the भागीदारी of अधिक than thirty-seven countries.
The forum was launched with the theme `` Promoting Democracy and Regional Development '' and twenty-five mayors सहित आंद्रे santini ( issy-les-moulineaux, फ़्रांस ), केविन foy ( चैपल हिल, us ), apirak kosayothin ( बैंकॉक, थाईलैंड ), uvais मोहम्मद emthiyas ( कोलोन, Sri Lanka ), and world experts such as Dr William H. A wonton ( also spelled wantan, wanton, or wuntun in ट्रांसक्रिप्शन इससे cantonese ; मंदारिन : húndùn ) is a प्रकार of पकौड़ी commonly मिला in a number of Chinese cuisines.
Many people were शामिल in the आविष्कार of रेडियो as we अभी know it.
Several possible methods of wireless communication were considered, including inductive और capacitive प्रेरण और हस्तांतरण through the मैदान, however the विधि प्रयुक्त लिये रेडियो आज exclusively involves the हस्तांतरण और रिसेप्शन of electromagnetic waves.
After जल्दी अटकलें on the विषय, प्रायोगिक कार्य on the कनेक्शन between विद्युत और चुंबकत्व began around 1820 साथ the work of Hans Christian Ørsted and continued with the work of André-Marie Ampère, Joseph Henry, and Michael Faraday.
These investigations culminated in the पूरा सिद्धान्त of विद्युत्चुम्बकत्व विकसित by जेम्स Clerk Maxwell.
This सिद्धान्त वर्णित the सैद्धांतिक आधार of the propagation of electromagnetic waves.
After मैक्सवेल 's सिद्धान्त थी प्रकाशित अनेक लोगों experimented साथ बेतार communication, some intentionally using Maxwell 's theory some not.
It is considered likely that the first intentional transmission of a signal by अर्थात् of इलेक्ट्रोमैग्नेटिक लहरें थी performed by दाउद एडवर्ड ह्यूजेस around 1880, हालांकि इस थी माना to be प्रेरण at the time.
The first systematic and unequivocal transmission of EM लहरें थी performed by heinrich रुडॉल्फ हर्ट्ज़ और वर्णित in papers प्रकाशित in 1887 और 1890.
Hertz famously माना ये परिणाम as होने of छोटी practical value.
After Hertz 's work many people were involved in the development of components and सिद्धान्त शामिल साथ the हस्तांतरण और रिसेप्शन of इलेक्ट्रोमैग्नेटिक waves.
Others, notably Guglielmo मार्कोनी, यहूद चिंतित साथ व्यावहारिक सुधार और the वाणिज्यिक अनुप्रयोग of रेडियो to बेतार telegraphy.
बाद on रेगिनाल्ड A. fessenden became the पहला to भेजें an ऑडियो सिग्नल by अर्थात् of electromagnetic waves.
Scurvy is a बीमारी resulting इससे a कमियां of विटामिन c, जिससे is जरूरी for the synthesis of collagen in humans.
The chemical name for vitamin C, ascorbic acid, is derived from the Latin नाम of स्कर्वी, scorbutus, जिससे भी provides the क्रियाशील scorbutic ( `` of, characterized by or having to do with scurvy '' ).
Scurvy often presents itself initially as लक्षण of malaise और lethargy, followed by गठन of धब्बे on the स्किन, spongy gums, and bleeding from the mucous membranes.
Spots are most abundant on the thighs and legs, and a व्यक्ति साथ the ailment looks पाले, feels उदास, और is partially immobilized.
As scurvy advances, there can be open, suppurating wounds, घाटा of दांत, पीलिया, ज्वर, न्यूरोपैथी और मौत.
Scurvy was at एक समय आम among sailors, pirates और अन्य सवार जहाजों at समुद्र longer than perishable फल और सब्जियां could be भंडारित ( subsisting बजाय तभी on cured and salted meats and dried grains ) and by soldiers similarly deprived of these foods for extended periods.
It was described by हिपोक्रेटिस ( c. 460 bc–c. 380 bc ), और हर्बल cures लिये स्कर्वी have महरूम ज्ञात in many native cultures since prehistory.
Scurvy was one of the limiting factors of समुद्री सफर, प्रायः हत्या विशाल संख्याएँ of the यात्री और क्रू on long-distance voyages.
This became a significant issue in Europe from the beginning of the आधुनिक era in the आयु of डिस्कवरी in the 15th सदी, continuing to play a significant role through World War I in the 20th century.
While today scurvy is known to be caused by a nutritional deficiency, until the isolation of विटामिन c और सीधा प्रमाण of इसके कड़ी to स्कर्वी in 1932, numerous theories और उपचार यहूद प्रस्तावित, often on little or no experimental data.
This inconsistency is attributed to the lack of vitamin c as a पृथक अवधारणा, an अक्षमता to reliably कड़ी अलग भोजन ( notably उपस्थित in भैस citrus, watercress, and organ meat ) to scurvy.
An additional concept required to understand स्कर्वी थी the degradation of विटामिन c by एक्सपोज़र to एयर और तांबे और अन्य परिवर्तन मेटल लवण ऐसे as those of आयरन, यूँ बदलना the कड़ी of भोजन to स्कर्वी over time.
उपचार by भैस खाना, विशेषकर citrus फल, थी periodically implemented, as it had been since antiquity.
However जबतक the 1930s, उपचार थी असंगत, साथ अनेक अप्रभावी treatments used into the 20th century.
It was a Scottish surgeon in the Royal Navy, James Lind who first proved it could be treated साथ citrus फल in प्रयोग he वर्णित in उसके 1753 किताब, a treatise of the स्कर्वी, हालांकि उसके सलाह थी नहीं implemented by the royal नेवी लिये अनेक decades.
In infants, scurvy is sometimes referred to as barlow 's बीमारी, नामित बाद सर थामस barlow, a अंग्रेजों चिकित्सक जो वर्णित it.
However, Barlow 's disease may भी refer to mitral वाल्व prolapse.
Other eponyms लिये स्कर्वी शामिल moeller 's बीमारी and Cheadle 's disease.
Scurvy does not occur in most animals because वे can synthesize उनके अपना विटामिन C.

Iron is a chemical element with the प्रतीक fe ( इससे ) और परमाणु क्रमांक 26.
It is a metal in the पहला परिवर्तन श्रेणी.
It is the most common element ( by mass ) forming the planet Earth as a पूरे, forming much of धरती 's बाहरी और भीतरी कोर.
It is the fourth most common तत्व in the धरती 's क्रस्ट.
Iron 's very common presence in rocky ग्रह जैसे धरती is due to इसके abundant उत्पादन as a परिणाम of संलयन in high-mass सितारों, जहाँ the उत्पादन of nickel-56 ( जिससे decays to the सबसे आम समस्थानिक of आयरन ) is the last nuclear fusion reaction that is exothermic.
इस कल्याणकारी रेडियोसक्रिय निकल to become the पिछला तत्व to be उत्पादित पहले पतन of a supernova leads to the explosive events that scatter this precursor radionuclide of iron abundantly into space.
Like other group 8 elements, iron exists in a wide range of ऑक्सीकरण राज्य, −2 to +6, हालांकि +2 और +3 हैं the सबसे आम.
Elemental iron occurs in meteoroids और अन्य कम ऑक्सीजन environments, लकिन is reactive to oxygen and water.
Fresh iron surfaces appear lustrous silvery-gray, लकिन oxidize in सामान्य एयर to दे hydrated आयरन आक्साइड, commonly known as rust.
Unlike many other metals which रूप passivating ऑक्साइड परतों, आयरन आक्साइड occupy अधिक आवाज़ than iron metal, and thus iron oxides flake off and expose fresh surfaces for corrosion.
Iron metal रै महरूम प्रयुक्त चूंकि प्राचीन टाइम्स, हालांकि तांबे alloys, जिससे have lower melting temperatures, were used first in history.
Pure iron is नरम ( softer than एल्युमिनियम ), लकिन is unobtainable by smelting.
The material is significantly hardened और strengthened by impurities इससे the smelting प्रक्रम, such as carbon.
A certain proportion of carbon ( between 0.002 % और 2.1 % ) produces स्टील, जिससे may be up to 1000 टाइम्स harder than pure iron.
crude आयरन मेटल is उत्पादित in धमाका furnaces, जहाँ अयस्क is घटाया by कोक to सुअर आयरन, which has a high carbon content.
Further refinement with oxygen reduces the carbon सामग्री to the सही proportion to मेक स्टील.
Steels and low carbon iron alloys with other metals ( alloy steels ) are by far the सबसे आम धातुओं in औद्योगिक उपयोग, due to उनके ग्रेट दायरा of वांछनीय गुण और the प्रचुरता of आयरन.
Iron chemical compounds, जिससे शामिल अमिश्रित और ferric यौगिकों, have many uses.
आयरन ऑक्साइड मिश्रित साथ एल्युमिनियम powder can be ignited to create a thermite reaction, used in welding and purifying ores.
It forms binary compounds with the हैलोजन्स और the chalcogens.
Among its organometallic यौगिकों is ferrocene, the पहला सैंडविच यौगिक खोजा.
Iron plays an important role in जीवविज्ञान, forming देवालय साथ आणविक ऑक्सीजन in हीमोग्लोबिन और myoglobin ; ये दो यौगिकों हैं आम oxygen transport proteins in vertebrates.
आयरन is भी the मेटल प्रयुक्त at the क्रियाशील साईट of अनेक महत्वपूर्ण रेडॉक्स एंजाइमों dealing साथ cellular respiration and oxidation and reduction in plants and animals.

He served three different शर्तें as स्पीकर of the संयुक्त राज्य हाउस of प्रतिनिधि और थी भी Secretary of State from 1825 to 1829.

Clay was a dominant फिगर in दोनो the पहला और दूसरी पार्टी systems.
As a leading युद्ध हॉक in 1812, he favored युद्ध साथ ब्रिटेन और निभाई a significant भूमिका in अग्रणी the nation to war in the War of 1812.

Clay was the foremost proponent of the American System, fighting for an बढ़ाएँ in tariffs to फोस्टर उद्योग in the संयुक्त राज्य, the उपयोग of संघीय funding to निर्माण और maintain अवसंरचना, and a strong national bank.
He opposed the annexation of Texas, fearing it होता इंजेक्ट the गुलामी समस्या into politics.
Clay भी opposed the mexican-american युद्ध और the `` manifest नियति `` policy of Democrats, which cost him votes in the close 1844 election.

A plantation owner, मिट्टी आयोजित स्लेव दौरान उसके आजीवन लकिन freed them in his Will.

The Chernobyl disaster (, Chornobylska Katastrofa – Chornobyl Catastrophe ) was a catastrophic nuclear accident कि occurred on 26 अप्रैल 1986 at the chernobyl नाभिकीय शक्ति संयंत्र in युक्त ( तब officially the यूक्रेनी ssr ), जिससे थी अंतर्गत the सीधा क्षेत्राधिकार of the सेंट्रल अधिकारियों of the Soviet Union.

The Chernobyl disaster is widely considered to have been the worst nuclear power plant accident in history, and is one of तभी दो वर्गीकृत as a स्तर 7 इवेंट on the अंतरराष्ट्रीय नाभिकीय इवेंट स्केल ( the अन्य होने the फुकुशिमा daiichi नाभिकीय विपत्ति in 2011 ).
The battle to contain the contamination and avert a वृहद प्रलय ultimately शामिल over 500,000 मजदूर और लागत an अनुमानित 18 billion rubles.
The official Soviet casualty count of 31 मौतों रै महरूम विवादित, और long-term प्रभाव ऐसे as cancers और deformities are still being accounted for.

The program is notable for targeting browser-hijacking विधि, बल्कि than relying on a डेटाबेस of ज्ञात spyware.
It scans a user 's कंप्यूटर जल्दी, और प्रदर्शक ब्राउजर hijacking स्थितियाँ, showing what entries are there.

HijackThis does not हटाएँ or detect स्पाइवेयर ; it सूचियाँ सबसे आम स्थितियाँ जहाँ ब्राउजर hijacking activity can occur.
ब्राउजर hijacking can कारण मैलवेयर to be संस्थापित on a computer.
On फ़रवरी 16, 2012, ट्रेंड सूक्ष्म released the hijackthis सोर्स code as open source and it is now available on the SourceForge site.

अमरीकी अखबारों reacted to the स्टैम्प अधिनियम with anger and predictions of the demise of journalism.
The Stamp Act 1765 ( short title Duties in अमरीकी colonies अधिनियम 1765 ; 5 जार्ज iii, c. 12 ) imposed a सीधा कर by the अंग्रेजों पार्लियामेंट specifically on the colonies of अंग्रेजों अमेरिका, और it जरूरी कि अनेक मुद्रित सामग्री in the colonies be produced on stamped paper produced in London, carrying an embossed revenue stamp.
These printed materials यहूद विधिक दस्तावेज़, मैगज़ीन, अखबारों और अनेक अन्य प्रकार of पेपर used throughout the colonies.
Like पिछला कर, the स्टैम्प कर था to be सशुल्क in मान्य अंग्रेजों करेंसी, not in colonial paper money.
The purpose of the tax was to help अदा लिये सैनिकों stationed in उत्तर अमेरिका बाद the अंग्रेजों victory in the Seven Years ' War.
The British government felt that the colonies यहूद the प्राथमिक beneficiaries of इस सैन्य उपस्थिति, और चाहिए pay at least a portion of the expense.
The स्टैम्प अधिनियम मिले ग्रेट प्रतिरोध in the colonies.
The colonies भेजा no प्रतिनिधि to पार्लियामेंट, और इसलिए था no influence over कया कर यहूद उठाया, how they were levied, or how they would be spent.
Many colonists considered it a violation of उनके अधिकारों as अंग्रेजो to be taxed बगैर उनके सहमति —consent that only the colonial legislatures could grant.
Colonial सभाओं भेजा याचिकाएं और विरोध.
The Stamp Act Congress held in New York City, reflecting the first significant संयुक्त औपनिवेशिक जवाब to कोई अंग्रेजों माप, also petitioned Parliament and the King.
लोकल विरोध समूह, led by औपनिवेशिक व्यापारियों और landowners, स्थापित connections through correspondence that created a loose coalition that extended from New England to Georgia.
Protests and demonstrations initiated by the बेटे of स्वतंत्रता प्रायः turned हिंसक और destructive as the masses became involved.
Very जल्द सब स्टैम्प कर वितरकों यहूद सहमे into resigning their commissions, and the tax was never effectively collected.
Opposition to the Stamp Act थी नहीं सीमित to the colonies.
British merchants and निर्माताओं, जिनकी निर्यात to the colonies यहूद threatened by औपनिवेशिक आर्थिक समस्याएं exacerbated by the tax, also pressured Parliament.
The Act was repealed on March 18, 1766 as a matter of expedience, लकिन पार्लियामेंट affirmed इसके शक्ति to legislate लिये the colonies “in सब मामले whatsoever” by भी गुजर the Declaratory Act.
There followed a श्रेणी of नई कर और regulations, likewise opposed by the colonists.
The episode played a major role in defining the grievances और enabling the व्यवस्थित औपनिवेशिक प्रतिरोध कि led to the American Revolution in 1775.

PT boats were a variety of torpedo-armed तेज़ आक्रमण शिल्प प्रयुक्त by the संयुक्त राज्य नेवी in संसार War II to attack larger surface ships.
`` PT '' is the US hull वर्गीकरण प्रतीक लिये `` पैट्रोल torpedo ''.
The pt नाव squadrons यहूद nicknamed `` the मच्छर fleet ''.
The Japanese पुकारा उन्हें `` शैतान नौकाएँ ''.
The असली pre– संसार युद्ध i torpedo नौकाएँ यहूद designed साथ `` displacement '' hulls.
वे विस्थापित up to 300 टन और the top speed was.
The PT boats used in World War II were built using the planing -type हल रूप विकसित लिये रेसिंग boats.
वे यहूद much छोटी ( 30–75 टन ) and faster ( 35–40 knots ).
Both types were designed to strike at larger warships साथ torpedoes, using अपेक्षाकृत ऊँची गति to मिलेंगी बंद, और छोटी आकार to avoid being spotted and hit by gunfire.
They were much less महंगी than विशाल warships.
PT boats यहूद much तेज़, छोटी, और सस्ता than conventional ( displacement hull ) vessels.
During World War II, American PT boats सगाई दुश्मन destroyers और numerous अन्य सतह शिल्प, ranging इससे छोटी boats to large supply ships.
PT boats also operated as gunboats विरूद्ध दुश्मन छोटी शिल्प, ऐसे as कराया barges प्रयुक्त by the जापानी शक्तियां for inter-island transport.
Good Friday is a religious holiday observed primarily by ईसाइयों commemorating the crucifixion of यीशु मसीह और उसके मौत at कलवारी.
The holiday is observed during Holy Week as भाग of the paschal triduum on the शुक्रवार preceding ईस्टर संडे, और may coincide साथ the Jewish observance of Passover.
It is also ज्ञात as पावन शुक्रवार, ग्रेट शुक्रवार, ब्लैक शुक्रवार, or ईस्टर शुक्रवार, though the latter properly refers to the Friday in Easter week.
Based on the details of the canonical gospels, the crucifixion of यीशु थी सबसे संभावित to have been on a Friday ( the day before the Sabbath ) ( ).
The estimated year of the Crucifixion is AD 33, by two different groups, and originally as AD 34 by इसहाक़ न्यूटन via the मतभेद between the biblical और जूलियन पंचांग और the crescent of the moon.
A third method, using a completely different खगोलीय दृष्टिकोण आधारित on a चंद्र crucifixion अंधेरा और ग्रहण मॉडल ( सतत साथ apostle पीटर 's सन्दर्भ to a `` चंद्रमा of रक्त '' in अधिनियमों 2:20 ), points to Friday, 3 April AD 33.

The attack on Pearl Harbor ( called Hawaii Operation or Operation AI by the Japanese इम्पीरियल सामान्य मुख्यालय ( आपरेशन z in नियोजन ) और the बैटल of पर्ल हार्बर ) थी a आश्चर्य सैन्य स्ट्राइक conducted by the इम्पीरियल जापानी नेवी विरूद्ध the संयुक्त States naval base at Pearl Harbor, Hawaii, on the morning of December 7, 1941 ( December 8 in Japan ).
From the standpoint of the defenders, the आक्रमण commenced at 7:48 a.m. हवाई Time.
The attack was intended as a निवारक कार्रवाई in अनुक्रम to रखना the u.S. प्रशांत बेड़े इससे दखल साथ सैन्य क्रियाएँ the साम्राज्य of जापानी थी नियोजन in southeast एशिया विरूद्ध विदेशी territories of the संयुक्त Kingdom, the Netherlands, and the United States.
The आधार थी attacked by 353 जापानी सेनानी, बमवर्षक और torpedo planes in दो लहरें, शुभारम्भ from six aircraft carriers.
All eight U.S. Navy battleships यहूद क्षतिग्रस्त, साथ चार होने sunk.
दो of ये यहूद बाद उठाया, और with the remaining four repaired, six battleships returned to service later in the war.
The जापानी भी sank or क्षतिग्रस्त तीन cruisers, तीन destroyers, an anti-aircraft training ship, and one minelayer.
188 u.S. वायुयान यहूद नष्ट ; 2,402 अमेरिकी were killed and 1,282 wounded.
Important base installations such as the power station, shipyard, maintenance, and fuel and torpedo storage facilities, as well as the पनडुब्बी पियर और मुख्यालय भवन ( भी घर of the प्रज्ञा खण्ड ) यहूद नहीं attacked.
Japanese losses were light : 29 aircraft and पाँच midget submarines खोया, और 65 servicemen मारे or wounded.
One जापानी नाविक थी captured.
The attack came as a profound shock to the American people और led सीधे to the अमरीकी प्रविष्टि into संसार युद्ध ii in दोनो the प्रशांत और यूरोपीय थिएटर.
The following day ( December 8 ), the संयुक्त राज्य घोषित युद्ध on Japan.
घरेलू support लिये non-interventionism, which had been strong, disappeared.
clandestine support of ब्रिटेन ( लिये उदाहरण the neutrality पैट्रोल ) was replaced by active alliance.
Subsequent operations by the u.S. prompted जर्मनी और इटली to घोषित युद्ध on the u.S. on दिसम्बर 11, जिससे थी reciprocated by the U.S. the same day.
There were numerous historical precedents लिये unannounced सैन्य कार्रवाई by जापानी.
However, the lack of any formal warning, particularly while negotiations were still apparently ongoing, led President फ्रैंकलिन D. रूज़वेल्ट to proclaim दिसम्बर 7, 1941, `` a तिथि जिससे होगा सजीव in infamy ``.

The United States presidential election of 1968 थी the 46th quadrennial अध्यक्षीय चुनाव, held on Tuesday, November 5, 1968.
The Republican nominee, पूर्व vice-president रिचर्ड निक्सन, जीती the चुनाव over the लोकतांत्रिक nominee, incumbent Vice-President Hubert Humphrey.
Nixon ran on a campaign that promised to restore विधि और अनुक्रम to the स्वदेश 's शहरों, torn by riots and crime.
Analysts have argued the election of 1968 is a realigning चुनाव as it permanently disrupted the नई सौदे गठबन्धन कि had dominated presidential politics for 36 years.
Coming four years after Democrat Lyndon B. Johnson जीती in a ऐतिहासिक भूस्खलन, the चुनाव देखी the लाज़िम अध्यक्ष मजबूर आउट of the race and a Republican elected for the first time in twelve years.
It was a wrenching national experience, conducted during a year of violence that included the assassination of civil rights leader Martin Luther King, Jr., and subsequent race riots across the nation, the assasination of लोकतांत्रिक अध्यक्षीय प्रत्याशी रॉबर्ट F. कैनेडी, फैली विपक्ष to the वियतनाम युद्ध आरपार विश्वविद्यालयों campuses, और हिंसक confrontations between पुलिस और anti-war प्रदर्शनकारियों at the 1968 लोकतांत्रिक नेशनल सम्मेलन as the Democratic party split again and again.
The election featured the strongest third party effort चूंकि 1912 by पूर्व अलबामा राज्यपाल जार्ज वालेस, a Democrat.
Because Wallace 's campaign opposed federal intervention in the South to end school segregation, he carried the गहन दक्षिण और भागा खूब in जातीय औद्योगिक जिले in the उत्तर.
This was the last चुनाव in जिससे नई यॉर्क था the सबसे मत in the चुनावी कॉलेज ( 43 votes ).
After the 1970 जनसांख्यिकी, कैलिफ़ोर्निया gained the सबसे चुनावी मत और रै remained the most populous state since then.
This is the latest election where a अध्यक्षीय टिकट जीती बगैर carrying the वाइस अध्यक्षीय प्रत्याशी 's घर state.

Kanji ( ; ) are the adopted logographic चाइनीज वर्ण ( hanzi ) कि हैं प्रयुक्त in the आधुनिक जापानी लिखने प्रणाली साथ साथ hiragana ( ひらがな, ), katakana ( カタカナ, ), Hindu-Arabic numerals, and the occasional use of the Latin alphabet.

A compass is a navigational instrument that shows दिशानिर्देश in a फ़्रेम of सन्दर्भ कि is stationary सापेक्ष to the surface of the earth.
The frame of reference defines the चार कार्डिनल दिशानिर्देश ( or अंक ) – उत्तर, दक्षिण, ईस्ट, और west.
Intermediate दिशानिर्देश हैं भी पारिभाषित.
प्रायः, a आरेख पुकारा a कम्पास रोज़, जिससे shows the दिशानिर्देश ( साथ their names usually abbreviated to initials ), is marked on the compass.
When the compass is in use, the rose is लकीर साथ the रियल दिशानिर्देश in the फ़्रेम of सन्दर्भ, so, लिये उदाहरण, the `` n '' चिह्नित on the रोज़ वाकई points to the north.
Frequently, in addition to the रोज़ or sometimes बजाय of it, कोण markings in डिग्री हैं दिखाया on the compass.
North corresponds to zero degrees, and the कोण बढ़ाएँ clockwise, so ईस्ट is 90 डिग्री, दक्षिण is 180, and west is 270.
These numbers allow the compass to show azimuths or बियरिंग, जिससे हैं commonly stated in इस संकेतन.
The magnetic compass was first invented as a device for भविष्यवाणी as जल्दी as the चाइनीज हान राजवंश ( चूंकि परिचय 206 BC ).
The compass was used in Song Dynasty China by the military for navigational orienteering by 1040-1044, और थी प्रयुक्त लिये मेरीटाइम नेविगेशन by 1111 to 1117.
The use of a कम्पास is अंकित in पश्चिमी यूरोपीय between 1187 और 1202, और in Persia in 1232.
The dry compass was invented in यूरोपीय around 1300.
This was supplanted in the जल्दी 20th सदी by the liquid-filled चुम्बकीय compass.
The Inca Empire or inka साम्राज्य ( quechua : tawantinsuyu ) थी the largest empire in pre-Columbian America.
The administrative, political and military बीच of the साम्राज्य थी स्तिथ in Cusco in modern-day Peru.
The Inca सभ्यता arose इससे the हाइलैंड्स of पेरू sometime in the जल्दी 13th century.
From 1438 to 1533, the Incas used a variety of methods, from conquest to peaceful assimilation, to incorporate a large portion of western South America, centered on the Andean mountain ranges, including, besides पेरू, विशाल भाग of आधुनिक इक्वाडोर, पश्चिमी और दक्षिण सेंट्रल बोलीविया, उत्तरपश्चिम अर्जेंटीना, उत्तर और सेंट्रल चिली, और दक्षिणी कोलंबिया into a राज्य comparable to the ऐतिहासिक empires of Eurasia.
The official language of the empire was Quechua, हालांकि सैंकड़ों of लोकल भाषाएं और dialects of quechua यहूद spoken.
The Inca referred to their empire as tawantinsuyu जिससे can be अनूदित as the चार regions or the चार संयुक्त Provinces.
There were many local forms of worship, most of them concerning local sacred `` Huacas ``, but the Inca leadership प्रोत्साहित the इबादत of inti —the सूर्य god—and imposed इसके प्रभुता ऊपर अन्य cults ऐसे as कि of pachamama.

The गुर्दे हैं अंगों कि serve अनेक अनिवार्य नियामक भूमिकाएँ in सबसे पशु, including vertebrates and some invertebrates.
They are essential in the urinary प्रणाली और भी serve homeostatic कृत्यों ऐसे as the विनियमन of इलेक्ट्रोलाइट्स, मेंटेनेंस of acid–base संतुलन, and regulation of blood pressure ( via maintaining salt and water balance ).
They serve the body as a प्राकृतिक फिल्टर of the रक्त, और हटाएँ wastes जिससे हैं diverted to the urinary bladder.
In producing urine, the kidneys excrete wastes ऐसे as यूरिया और अमोनियम, और वे हैं भी जिम्मेदार लिये the reabsorption of water, glucose, and amino acids.

Located at the rear of the abdominal cavity in the retroperitoneum, the गुर्दे प्राप्त रक्त इससे the युग्म renal arteries, and drain into the paired renal veins.
Each kidney excretes urine into a ureter, itself a युग्म ढांचा कि empties into the urinary ब्लैडर.
Renal physiology is the study of गुर्दा फलन, जबकि nephrology is the चिकित्सा specialty चिंतित with kidney diseases.
Diseases of the गुर्दा हैं विविध, लकिन individuals with kidney disease frequently display characteristic clinical features.

Various cancers of the गुर्दा मौजूद ; the सबसे आम वयस्क renal cancer is renal cell carcinoma.
Cancers, cysts, और कुछ अन्य renal शर्तें can be प्रबंधित साथ हटाना of the गुर्दा, or nephrectomy.
जब renal फलन, measured by glomerular filtration rate, is persistently poor, dialysis and kidney transplantation may be treatment options.
Although they are not severely नुकसानदेह, गुर्दा पत्थरों can be दुखद और a nuisance.

Negligence ( Lat. negligentia, इससे neglegere, to उपेक्षा, वस्तुतः `` नहीं to चुनें up कुछ '' ) is a विफलता to कसरत the care that a reasonably prudent person would exercise in like circumstances.
The क्षेत्रफल of अपकृत्य विधि ज्ञात as लापरवाही involves harm caused by carelessness, not intentional harm.
According to jay M. feinman of the rutgers विश्वविद्यालयों School of Law ;
`` The core idea of लापरवाही is कि लोगों चाहिए कसरत उचित परवाह जब वे अधिनियम by लेने खाता of the संभावित नुक़सान कि वे might foreseeably cause harm to other people. ''
`` those who go personally or bring property where they know that they or it may come into टक्कर साथ the व्यक्तियों or प्रॉपर्टी of अन्य have by विधि a ड्यूटी डाल upon उन्हें to उपयोग उचित परवाह और कौशल to avoid ऐसे a collision. ''
Fletcher v Rylands ( [ 1866 ] lr 1 ex 265 )
Through civil litigation, if an घायल व्यक्ति proves कि another व्यक्ति acted negligently to कारण उनके चोट, वे can recover damages to compensate for their harm.
Proving a मामला लिये लापरवाही can potentially entitle the घायल अभियोक्ता to मुआवजे लिये harm to their body, property, mental well-being, financial status, or intimate relationships.
However, because negligence cases are very fact-specific, this सामान्य परिभाषा करता नहीं fully बताइये the अवधारणा of जब the विधि होगा आवश्यकता एक व्यक्ति to compensate another for losses caused by accidental injury.
Further, the विधि of लापरवाही at आम विधि is तभी एक पहलू of the law of liability.
Although resulting damages must be सिद्ध in अनुक्रम to रिकवर मुआवजे in a लापरवाही कार्रवाई, the प्रकृति और extent of those क्षतिपूर्ति are not the primary focus of negligence cases.

A mole can be either subdermal ( under the skin ) or a pigmented विकास on the स्किन, formed ज़्यादातर of a प्रकार of cell known as a melanocyte.
The high concentration of the body’s pigmenting एजेंट, मेलेनिन, is जिम्मेदार लिये उनके अंधेरा रंग.
Moles are a सदस्य of the परिवार of स्किन lesions ज्ञात as nevi.
The comprehensive metabolic panel, or chemical स्क्रीन, ( cmp ; cpt कोड 80053 ) is a फलक of 14 रक्त परीक्षण जिससे serves as an आरंभिक व्यापक चिकित्सा स्क्रीनिंग tool.
The CMP provides a rough check of गुर्दा फलन, जिगर फलन, और electrolyte और fluid balance, but it is far from perfect.
असामान्य मान इससे a cbc may be a परिणाम of गलत positives और यूँ the cbc may need to be दोहराया लिये a patient ( or replaced with a more specific test ).
The CMP is an expanded संस्करण of the मौलिक metabolic फलक ( bmp ), जिससे करता नहीं शामिल जिगर tests.
A CMP ( or BMP ) can be ordered as part of a routine physical examination, or may be प्रयुक्त to मॉनिटर a रोगी साथ a दीर्घकालिक बीमारी, ऐसे as मधुमेह mellitus or hypertension.

Natural gas is a naturally occurring हाइड्रोकार्बन गैस मिश्रण consisting primarily of मिथेन, लकिन commonly सहित varying amounts of other hydrocarbons, carbon dioxide, nitrogen, and hydrogen sulfide.
Natural गैस is an उर्जा सोर्स प्रायः प्रयुक्त लिये हीटिंग, कुकिंग, और electricity generation.
It is also used as fuel for vehicles and as a रासायनिक फर्टिलाइजर in the manufacture of प्लास्टिक और अन्य commercially महत्वपूर्ण organic chemicals.
Natural गैस is मिला in गहन भूमिगत प्राकृतिक चट्टान formations or संबद्ध साथ अन्य हाइड्रोकार्बन टंकी in कोयले beds and as methane clathrates.
Petroleum is भी another संसाधन मिला in निकटता to and with natural gas.
Most natural gas was created over समय by दो mechanisms : biogenic और thermogenic.
Biogenic गैस is निर्मित by methanogenic जीवों in marshes, bogs, landfills, and shallow sediments.
Deeper in the earth, at greater temperature और दबाव, thermogenic गैस is निर्मित इससे दफ्न सशुल्क सामग्री.
पहले प्राकृतिक गैस can be प्रयुक्त as a ईंधन, it जरूर undergo प्रसंस्करण to हटाएँ impurities, सहित water, to meet the specifications of marketable natural gas.
The by-products of प्रसंस्करण शामिल इथेन, प्रोपेन, butanes, pentanes, और उच्चतर आणविक वज़न hydrocarbons, हाइड्रोजन sulfide ( जिससे may be converted into pure sulfur ), carbon dioxide, water vapor, and sometimes helium and nitrogen.
Natural gas is often informally referred to बस as गैस, विशेषकर जब compared to other energy sources such as oil or coal.

the platypus ( ornithorhynchus anatinus ) is a semiaquatic स्तनधारी endemic to eastern Australia, including Tasmania.
Together with the four species of एकिडना, it is एक of the पाँच extant प्रजाति of monotremes, the तभी स्तनधारियों कि lay eggs instead of giving birth.
It is the एकमात्र जीना प्रतिनिधि of इसके परिवार ( ornithorhynchidae ) और genus ( ornithorhynchus ), हालांकि a number of related species have been found in the fossil record.
The unusual appearance of इस egg-laying, बतख -billed, बीवर -tailed, otter -footed स्तनधारी मनोरथ यूरोपीय naturalists जब वे पहला encountered it, साथ some considering it an elaborate fraud.
It is one of the few venomous mammals, the पुरूष platypus having a spur on the हिन्द पैर कि delivers a venom सक्षम of causing severe pain to humans.
The unique features of the platypus मेक it an महत्वपूर्ण विषय in the पढ़ाई of विकासवादी जीवविज्ञान और a recognisable और iconic प्रतीक of ऑस्ट्रेलिया ; it रै appeared as a mascot at national events and is featured on the reverse of its 20-cent coin.
The platypus is the एनिमल emblem of the राज्य of नई दक्षिण वेल्स.
Until the early 20th सदी, it थी hunted लिये इसके फर, लकिन it is अभी सुरक्षित throughout its range.
Although captive breeding programmes have था तभी सीमित कामयाबी और the platypus is vulnerable to the प्रभाव of प्रदूषण, it is not under any immediate threat.

The North American Free Trade Agreement ( nafta ) is an अनुबंध हस्ताक्षरित by कनाडा, मैक्सिको, और the संयुक्त राज्य, बनाना a trilateral व्यापार bloc in North America.
The अनुबंध आए into फ़ोर्स on January 1, 1994.
It superseded the canada–united राज्य फ़्री व्यापार अनुबंध between the u.S., कनाडा, और Mexico
NAFTA has two supplements : the North American Agreement on Environmental सहयोग ( naaec ) और the उत्तर अमरीकी अनुबंध on मजदूर सहयोग ( naalc ).
Thermal comfort is the condition of mind that expresses satisfaction with the थर्मल पर्यावरण और is assessed by subjective मूल्यांकन ( ansi / ASHRAE Standard 55 ).
maintaining इस मानक of थर्मल सुकून लिये occupants of इमारतें or अन्य enclosures is एक of the महत्वपूर्ण लक्ष्य of HVAC ( heating, ventilation, and air conditioning ) design engineers.
The Predicted Mean Vote ( PMV ) model stands among the सबसे पहचाना थर्मल सुकून मॉडल.
It was developed using principles of heat balance and प्रायोगिक आंकड़ा एकत्रित in a नियंत्रित जलवायु कक्ष अंतर्गत स्थिर राज्य शर्तें.
Because the PMV model was derived from data एकत्रित in a नियंत्रित जलवायु, it is नहीं उपयुक्त लिये अनुप्रयोग in naturally हवादार स्पेसेस जिससे प्रायः have ऊँची स्तर of एयर movement.
This shortcoming motivated the विकास of a परिवार of अनुभवजन्य सांख्यिकीय मॉडल of थर्मल सुकून in naturally हवादार spaces known as adaptive models.
Adaptive models of थर्मल सुकून consider occupants as dynamically interacting साथ उनके पर्यावरण, और controlling their thermal comfort by means of clothing or window-opening and closing.
This is in contrast to thermal comfort in sealed buildings, in जिससे occupants अनुभव the पर्यावरण passively.
Thermal comfort is affected by heat conduction, convection, विकिरण, और evaporative ऊष्मा घाटा.
Thermal comfort is maintained when the heat generated by इंसान चयापचय is अनुमत to dissipate, यूँ maintaining थर्मल संतुलन साथ the surroundings.
it रै महरूम long पहचाना कि the सनसनी of अहसास hot or ठंडा is not just dependent on air temperature alone.
Thermal comfort calculations according to ansi/ashrae मानक 55 can be freely performed साथ the cbe थर्मल Comfort Tool for ASHRAE-55.
Durante degli Alighieri, simply referred to as दांते (, ; ; c. 1265–1321 ), थी a प्रमुख इतालवी कवि of the मध्य Ages.

मुख्यालय ( कोबे, Japan )
( ) is a टायर और रबर कम्पनी आधारित in Japan.
It is भाग of the sumitomo समूह.
The company traces इसके origins to 1909, जब the sumitomo समूह बना an निवेश in dunlop जापानी, the newly formed Japanese subsidiary of the British company Dunlop Rubber.
Over the years Sumitomo and Dunlop developed a close कारोबार संबंध, और in 1963 the sumitomo समूह acquired कंट्रोल of dunlop जापानी और renamed it sumitomo रबर उद्योग Ltd.
In 1985, when Dunlop Rubber was taken over by BTR plc, the company acquired the ऑटोमोबाइल टायर एसेट of dunlop, सहित the सही to उपयोग the dunlop ब्रांड on ऑटोमोबाइल tires.
The acquisition किया नहीं शामिल the us और ऑस्ट्रेलियाई व्यवसायों, जिससे यहूद separately स्वामित्व, लकिन in 1986 sumitomo भी acquired the Dunlop Tire Corporation of the US from its management.
In 1997, sumitomo formed a संयुक्त venture साथ goodyear टायर और रबर कम्पनी, by जिससे goodyear और sumitomo सहमत to manufacture टायर for each other 's markets, including Dunlop branded tires.
As भाग of the अनुबंध, goodyear acquired 75 % रूचि in dunlop टायर, the uk company which Sumitomo had formed, and in Dunlop Tire Corporation.
goodyear और sumitomo भी बना investments in each other.
Today, the company makes a wide range of रबर आधारित उत्पाद, सहित ऑटोमोबाइल tires, golf balls and tennis balls.

The Alps हैं एक of the ग्रेट पहाड़ दायरा प्रणालियों of यूरोपीय stretching लगभग आरपार आठ अल्पाइन देशों from Austria and Slovenia in the east, Switzerland, Liechtenstein, Germany, France to the west and Italy and Monaco to the south.
The mountains यहूद formed over सैंकड़ों of लाखो of सालो as the अफ़्रीकी और यूरेशियाई tectonic plates collided.
Extreme shortening caused by the इवेंट resulted in समुद्री sedimentary रॉक्स उठती by thrusting and folding into high mountain peaks such as Mont Blanc and the Matterhorn.
Mont Blanc spans the French–Italian किनारा, और at is the उच्चतम पहाड़ in the ऐल्प्स.
the अल्पाइन प्रदेश क्षेत्रफल contains many peaks higher than, known as the `` four-thousanders ``.
The altitude and size of the range affects the climate in Europe ; in the kyu वर्षण स्तर vary greatly और climatic शर्तें consist of पृथक zones.
Wildlife such as ibex सजीव in the उच्चतर चोटियों to elevations of, और पौधे ऐसे as edelweiss grow in rocky areas in lower elevations as well as in higher elevations.
Evidence of इंसान habitation in the ऐल्प्स goes वापस to the paleolithic era.
A mummified man, determined to be 5,000 years old, was खोजा on a हिमानी at the austrian–italian किनारा in 1991.
By the 6th century BC, the सेल्टिक la tène संस्कृति थी खूब स्थापित.
hannibal may have crossed the ऐल्प्स साथ a herd of elephants, and the Romans had settlements in the region.
In 1800 Napoleon crossed एक of the पहाड़ passes with an army of 40,000.
The 18th and 19th centuries saw an influx of naturalists, लेखक, और कलाकारों, in particular the Romantics, followed by the golden age of alpinism as mountaineers began to ascend the peaks.
In World War II the Third Reich invaded the Alpine countries, with the एक्सेप्शन of स्विट्ज़रलैंड और liechtenstein ; एडोल्फ हिटलर रखा a base of operation in the Bavarian Alps throughout the war.
The Alpine प्रदेश रै a दमदार सांस्कृतिक पहचान.
The traditional culture of farming, cheesemaking, and woodworking still exists in अल्पाइन गांवों, हालांकि the पर्यटक उद्योग began to grow जल्दी in the 20th सदी और विस्तारित greatly बाद संसार युद्ध II to become the dominant industry by the end of the century.
The Winter Olympic Games have been hosted in the स्विस, फ्रेंच, इतालवी, आस्ट्रिया and German Alps.
At present the region is घर to 14 लाख लोगों और रै 120 लाख annual visitors.

Basque ( endonym :, ) is the ancestral भाषा of the बास्क लोगों, जो inhabit the बास्क देश, a प्रदेश spanning an क्षेत्रफल in northeastern Spain and southwestern France.
It is spoken by 27 % of Basques in सब territories ( 714,136 आउट of 2,648,998 ).
Of these, 663,035 live in the स्पेनी भाग of the बास्क देश और the बाकी 51,100 live in the French part.
In academic discussions of the distribution of Basque in स्पेन और फ़्रांस, it is प्रथागत to refer to तीन प्राचीन प्रांतों in फ़्रांस और चार Spanish provinces.
Native speakers are concentrated in a contiguous area including parts of the Spanish autonomous समुदायों of the बास्क देश और नावारा और in the पश्चिमी हाफ of the फ्रेंच département of Pyrénées-Atlantiques.
The Basque Autonomous Community is an administrative entity within the binational ethnographic बास्क देश incorporating the परंपरागत स्पेनी प्रांतों of biscay, gipuzkoa, और álava, जिससे retain उनके existence as politico-administrative divisions.
These provinces and many areas of Navarre are heavily populated by ethnic Basques, but Basque was, at least until the 1990s, नहीं बोला as a देशी भाषा in सबसे of álava, पश्चिमी भाग of biscay और सेंट्रल और दक्षिणी क्षेत्रों of नावारा, either क्युकी it था महरूम replaced by स्पेनी साथ the सदियां, in कुछ क्षेत्रों, or क्युकी it had never been spoken there, in other areas.
In southwestern France, the प्राचीन basque-populated प्रांतों यहूद labourd, निम्नतर नावारा, and Soule.
They and other regions were consolidated into a single département in 1790 अंतर्गत the नाम basses-pyrénées, a नाम जिससे persisted जबतक 1970.
A standardized form of the बास्क भाषा, पुकारा euskara batua, थी विकसित by the बास्क Language Academy in the late 1960s.
Euskara Batua was created so that Basque language could be used—and easily समझा by सब बास्क speakers—in औपचारिक परिस्थितियों ( शिक्षा, द्रव्यमान मीडिया, साहित्य ), और इस is इसके प्रमुख use today.
The role of this standard Basque language depends on the भाषाई शैक्षणिक मॉडल of प्रत्येक region and each school.
In most areas of the Spanish Basque Country, the शैक्षणिक मॉडल d, जहाँ सब विषय हैं सिखाया in बास्क, मगर `` स्पेनी भाषा और साहित्य '' ( जिससे is सिखाया in स्पेनी ) is now the predominant model.
In फ़्रांस, the बास्क भाषा स्कूल seaska और the संघ लिये a दुभाषिया ( बास्क और फ्रेंच ) schooling ikasbi मिलें a wide range of Basque language educational needs up to the Sixth Form, while often struggling to surmount financial and administrative constraints.
Apart from this standardized संस्करण, वहीँ हैं पाँच प्रमुख बास्क dialects : bizkaian, gipuzkoan, और अपर navarrese in Spain, and Navarrese–Lapurdian and Zuberoan ( in France ).
Although they take their names from the mentioned historic provinces, the dialect सीमाएँ हैं नहीं congruent साथ प्रांत सीमाएँ.
The President, Directors and Company, of the बैंको of the संयुक्त राज्य, commonly ज्ञात as the पहला बैंको of the संयुक्त राज्य, थी a सेंट्रल बैंको, चार्टर्ड लिये a पद of बीस सालो, by the United States Congress on February 25, 1791.
स्थापना of the बैंको थी शामिल in a three-part विस्तार of संघीय फिस्कल और मौद्रिक शक्ति ( साथ साथ a federal mint and excise taxes ) championed by Alexander Hamilton, first Secretary of the Treasury.
Hamilton believed a central bank was necessary to stabilize and improve the nation 's क्रेडिट, और to improve हैंडलिंग of the वित्तीय कारोबार of the संयुक्त राज्य सरकारी अंतर्गत the newly enacted Constitution.
Officially proposed to the first session of the First कॉंग्रेस in 1790, हैमिल्टन 's बैंको faced फैली प्रतिरोध इससे opponents of increased federal power.
Secretary of State Thomas Jefferson and James Madison led the opposition, which claimed that the बैंको थी असंवैधानिक, और कि it benefited व्यापारियों और निवेशकों at the व्यय of the बहुमत of the जनसांख्यिकी.
The First Bank building is now a नेशनल ऐतिहासिक लैंडमार्क स्तिथ in फिलाडेल्फिया, पेन्सिलवेनिया भीतर स्वतंत्रता National Historical Park.

in आणविक जीवविज्ञान, इंसान chorionic gonadotropin ( hcg ) is a हार्मोन उत्पादित by the fertilized egg after conception.

A given name, in Western contexts often referred to as a first name, is a personal name that specifies and differentiates between सदस्यों of a समूह of individuals, विशेषकर in a परिवार, सब of जिनकी सदस्यों प्रायः share the वही परिवार नाम ( उपनाम ).
A given name is purposefully given, प्रायः by a चाइल्ड 's अभिभावक at or निकट जनम, in कंट्रास्ट to an inherited one such as a family name.
A दिए नाम is sometimes legally changed through a name change.
Given names are often used in a परिचित और दोस्ताना manner in informal situations.
In more formal situations the उपनाम is प्रयुक्त बजाय, जबतक it is जरुरी to फर्क between लोगों साथ the same surname.
The idiom `` on a first-name आधार '' ( or `` on first-name शर्तें '' ) alludes to the अपनेपन of संबोधित another by a given name.
The western style of having दोनो a परिवार नाम ( उपनाम ) और a दिए नाम is far from universal.
In many देशों it is आम लिये ordinary लोगों to have तभी one name ( a mononym ).
Hydrochloric acid is a clear, colourless solution of हाइड्रोजन chloride ( h cl ) in जल.
It is a highly क्षयकारी, दमदार खनिज एसिड साथ अनेक औद्योगिक uses.
हाइड्रोक्लोरिक एसिड is मिला naturally in gastric acid.
Historically called muriatic एसिड, और आत्माओं of नमक, हाइड्रोक्लोरिक एसिड थी उत्पादित इससे vitriol ( sulfuric acid ) and common salt.
It first appeared दौरान the पुनर्जागरण, और तब it थी प्रयुक्त by chemists ऐसे as glauber, प्रीस्टलि and Davy in their scientific research.
With major production starting in the Industrial Revolution, hydrochloric acid is used in the chemical industry as a रासायनिक अभिकर्मक in the large-scale उत्पादन of विनाइल chloride लिये पीवीसी प्लास्टिक, और mdi / tdi लिये polyurethane.
It has numerous smaller-scale अनुप्रयोग, सहित household सफ़ाई, उत्पादन of जिलेटिन और अन्य खाना एडिटिव, descaling, and leather processing.
परिचय 20 लाख टन of हाइड्रोक्लोरिक acid are produced annually.
Wheat ( triticum spp. ) is a खाद्यान्न अनाज, originally इससे the levant प्रदेश of the निकट ईस्ट and Ethiopian Highlands, but now cultivated worldwide.
In 2010, world production of wheat was 651 लाख टन, बनाना it the तीसरा most-produced खाद्यान्न बाद मक्का ( 844 million tons ) and rice ( 672 million tons ).
Wheat was the second most-produced cereal in 2009 ; world production in कि साल थी 682 लाख टन, बाद मक्का ( 817 लाख टन ), और साथ राइस as a बंद तीसरा ( 679 million tons ).
This grain is grown on अधिक जमीन क्षेत्रफल than कोई अन्य वाणिज्यिक food.
World व्यापार in गेहूं is वृहद than लिये सब other crops combined.
Globally, wheat is the leading source of vegetable protein in human food, having a higher protein content than soybeans or the अन्य प्रमुख cereals, मक्का ( मकई ) or राइस.
In terms of total production tonnages प्रयुक्त लिये खाना, it is फिलहाल दूसरी to राइस as the प्रमुख इंसान खाना क्रॉप और ahead of मक्का, बाद allowing for maize 's more extensive use in animal feeds.
Wheat was a key factor enabling the emergence of city-based societies at the प्रारंभ of सभ्यता क्युकी it थी एक of the पहला फसलों कि could be easily cultivated on a विशाल स्केल, और had the additional advantage of yielding a harvest that provides long-term storage of food.
Wheat contributed to the emergence of city-states in the fertile crescent, सहित the Babylonian and Assyrian empires.
Wheat grain is a staple food used to make flour for leavened, flat and steamed breads, biscuits, कुकीज़, cakes, नाश्ता खाद्यान्न, पास्ता, नूडल्स, couscous और लिये fermentation to मेक बियर, अन्य alcoholic पेय, or biofuel.
Wheat is planted to a limited extent as a forage क्रॉप लिये पशुधन, और इसके स्ट्रॉ can be प्रयुक्त as a construction material for roofing thatch.

the धर्मं व्हील, प्रायः प्रयुक्त to represent the Noble Eightfold Path
The Noble eightfold पाथ (, ) is एक of the प्रिंसिपल शिक्षाओं of the बुद्ध, जो वर्णित it as the रास्ता अग्रणी to the cessation of कष्ट ( dukkha ) and the achievement of self-awakening.
It is used to develop insight into the true प्रकृति of phenomena ( or वास्तविकता ) और to eradicate लोभ, द्वेष, and delusion.
The Noble Eightfold Path is the चौथी of the बुद्ध 's चार प्रतिष्ठित सच्चाई ; the पहला तत्व of the प्रतिष्ठित eightfold पाथ is, in turn, an understanding of the Four Noble Truths.
It is also known as the Middle पाथ or मध्य रास्ता.
All eight elements of the Path begin with the word `` right '', which translates the शब्द samyañc ( in संस्कृत ) or sammā ( in Pāli ).
These denote completion, एकजुटता, और coherence, और can भी सुझाएँ the senses of `` perfect '' or `` ideal ''.
'Samma ' is also translated as `` wholesome '', `` हिकमत '' और `` skillful ''.
In बौद्ध प्रतीकवाद, the प्रतिष्ठित eightfold पाथ is प्रायः represented by अर्थात् of the धर्मं व्हील ( dharmachakra ), जिनकी आठ तीलियां represent the eight elements of the path.
The Grammy Award for Song of the Year is an honor प्रस्तुत at the ग्रैमी पुरस्कार, a रस्म कि थी स्थापित in 1958 और originally पुकारा the Gramophone Awards.

Economics is the सोशल विज्ञान कि analyzes the उत्पादन, वितरण, and consumption of goods and services.
The term economics comes from the Ancient Greek ( ', `` management of a household, प्रशासन '' ) इससे ( ', `` हाउस '' ) + ( ', `` custom '' or `` law '' ), hence `` rules of the house ( hold ) ''.
Political economy was the earlier name for the subject, but economists in the लेट 19th सदी सुझाया `` अर्थशास्त्र '' as a shorter पद लिये `` आर्थिक विज्ञान '' कि भी avoided a सीमित political-interest connotation and as similar in form to `` mathematics ``, `` ethics '', and so forth.
A focus of the विषय is कैसा आर्थिक एजेंटों व्यवहार or interact और कैसा economies work.
Consistent with this, a primary textbook भेद is between microeconomics और macroeconomics.
Microeconomics examines the behavior of basic तत्व in the अर्थव्यवस्था, सहित व्यक्तिगत एजेंटों ( ऐसे as households और firms or as खरीदार and sellers ) and markets, and their interactions.
Macroeconomics analyzes the entire economy और मुद्दे affecting it, सहित बेरोजगारी, महंगाई, आर्थिक growth, and monetary and fiscal policy.
Other broad distinctions include those between धनात्मक अर्थशास्त्र ( describing `` कया is '' ) और normative अर्थशास्त्र ( वकालत `` कया ought to be '' ) ; between आर्थिक सिद्धान्त और लागू अर्थशास्त्र ; between तर्कसंगत और behavioral अर्थशास्त्र ; और between मुख्यधारा economics ( more `` orthodox '' and dealing with the `` rationality-individualism-equilibrium nexus '' ) and heterodox economics ( more `` radical '' and dealing with the `` institutions-history-social structure nexus '' ).
Economic analysis may be applied throughout society, as in business, finance, स्वास्थ्य परवाह, और सरकारी, लकिन भी to ऐसे विविध विषय as अपराधों, शिक्षा, the परिवार, विधि, राजनीती, religion, social institutions, war, and science.
At the फेरे of the 21st सदी, the expanding डोमेन of अर्थशास्त्र in the सोशल sciences has been described as economic imperialism.
An increasing क्रमांक of अर्थशास्त्रियों have पुकारा लिये increased जोर on पर्यावरणीय sustainability ; this area of research is known as Ecological economics.

Household income is a measure commonly प्रयुक्त by the संयुक्त राज्य सरकारी और निजी institutions.

As households tend to share a समान आर्थिक कॉन्टेक्स्ट, the उपयोग of household income remains among the most widely accepted measures of income.

Section 8 of the Housing Act of 1937 ( ), often simply known as खण्ड 8, as repeatedly amended, authorizes the भुगतान of rental आवास सहायता to private landlords on behalf of approximately 3.1 million low-income households.
It operates through अनेक कार्यक्रम, the largest of जिससे, the आवास चुनाव वाउचर कार्यक्रम, pays a large portion of the rents and utilities of about 2.1 million households.
The US Department of Housing and शहरी विकास manages the खण्ड 8 programs.
The Housing Choice Voucher Program provides `` tenant-based '' rental सहायता, so a किरायेदार can मूव इससे एक unit of at least minimum housing quality to another.
It भी allows individuals to लागू उनके मासिक वाउचर towards the खरीदें of a home, with over $ 17 billion going towards such purchases each year ( from ncsha.org analysis ).

खण्ड 8 भी authorizes a किस्में of `` project-based '' rental सहायता कार्यक्रम, अंतर्गत जिससे the मालिक reserves कुछ or सब of the इकाई in a भवन लिये low-income किरायेदारों, in वापसी for a Federal government guarantee to make up the difference between the tenant 's contribution and the rent for 1 cent in the owner 's contract with the government.
A tenant who leaves a subsidized प्रोजेक्ट होगा खोना अभिगम to the project-based रियायत.
